list page component\nexport default function Courses() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  const { courses, isLoading, isError, mutate } = useCourses();\n  \n  // State for create course dialog\n  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [courseData, setCourseData] = useState({\n    course_id: '',\n    semester: '',\n  });\n  \n  // State for delete course dialog\n  const [deleteDialogOpen, setDeleteDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [courseToDelete, setCourseToDelete] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Generate semester options (current semester + 2 future semesters)\n  const getSemesterOptions = () => {\n    const now = new Date();\n    const year = now.getFullYear();\n    const month = now.getMonth();\n    \n    let semesters = [];\n    let currentYear = year;\n    let seasons = ['Spring', 'Summer', 'Fall'];\n    \n    // Determine current season\n    let currentSeasonIndex;\n    if (month < 4) currentSeasonIndex = 0; // Spring\n    else if (month < 8) currentSeasonIndex = 1; // Summer\n    else currentSeasonIndex = 2; // Fall\n    \n    // Add current semester and next 4 semesters\n    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n      const seasonIndex = (currentSeasonIndex + i) % 3;\n      const yearOffset = Math.floor((currentSeasonIndex + i) / 3);\n      semesters.push(`${seasons[seasonIndex]} ${currentYear + yearOffset}`);\n    }\n    \n    return semesters;\n  };\n  \n  const semesterOptions = getSemesterOptions();\n  \n  // Handle creating a new course\n  const handleCreateCourse = async () => {\n    try {\n      await courseService.createCourse(courseData.semester, {\n        course_id: courseData.course_id,\n        semester: courseData.semester,\n        instructors: [], // Will be populated with current user\n      });\n      \n      // Refresh course list\n      mutate();\n      \n      // Reset form and close dialog\n      setCourseData({\n        course_id: '',\n        semester: '',\n      });\n      setCreateDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Course created successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error creating course:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to create course');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle deleting a course\n  const handleDeleteCourse = async () => {\n    if (!courseToDelete) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await courseService.deleteCourse(courseToDelete.course_id, courseToDelete.semester);\n      \n      // Refresh course list\n      mutate();\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n      setCourseToDelete(null);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Course deleted successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error deleting course:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to delete course');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Open delete confirmation dialog\n  const openDeleteDialog = (course, event) => {\n    event.stopPropagation();\n    setCourseToDelete(course);\n    setDeleteDialogOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Navigate to course detail page\n  const navigateToCourse = (course) => {\n    router.push(`/course/${course.course_id}?semester=${course.semester}`);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle form input changes\n  const handleInputChange = (event) => {\n    const { name, value } = event.target;\n    setCourseData({\n      ...courseData,\n      [name]: value,\n    });\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box sx={{ py: 3 }}>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Courses\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <Button\n          variant=\"contained\"\n          color=\"primary\"\n          startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n          onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}\n        >\n          Create Course\n        </Button>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {isError && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          Failed to load courses. Please try again.\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      {isLoading ? (\n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((item) => (\n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={item}>\n              <CardSkeleton height={180} />\n            </Grid>\n          ))}\n        </Grid>\n      ) : courses && courses.length > 0 ? (\n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          {courses.map((course) => (\n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={`${course.course_id}-${course.semester}`}>\n              <CourseCard>\n                <CardActionArea onClick={() => navigateToCourse(course)}>\n                  <CourseCardContent>\n                    <CourseCardHeader>\n                      <Typography variant=\"h6\" component=\"h2\" noWrap>\n                        {course.course_id}\n                      </Typography>\n                      <IconButton\n                        size=\"small\"\n                        color=\"error\"\n                        aria-label=\"delete course\"\n                        onClick={(e) => openDeleteDialog(course, e)}\n                      >\n                        <DeleteIcon fontSize=\"small\" />\n                      </IconButton>\n                    </CourseCardHeader>\n                    \n                    <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                      {course.semester}\n                    </Typography>\n                    \n                    <Divider sx={{ my: 1.5 }} />\n                    \n                    <InstructorsList>\n                      <PersonIcon />\n                      <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                        {course.instructors.length} {course.instructors.length === 1 ? 'Instructor' : 'Instructors'}\n                      </Typography>\n                    </InstructorsList>\n                  </CourseCardContent>\n                </CardActionArea>\n              </CourseCard>\n            </Grid>\n          ))}\n        </Grid>\n      ) : (\n        <NoCoursesBox>\n          <SchoolIcon sx={{ fontSize: 60, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 2 }} />\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n            No Courses Found\n          </Typography>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" paragraph>\n            You don't have any courses yet. Create your first course to get started.\n          </Typography>\n          <Button\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n            onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}\n          >\n            Create Course\n          </Button>\n        </NoCoursesBox>\n      )}\n      \n      {/* Create Course Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={createDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setCreateDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Create New Course</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <DialogContentText sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n            Enter the course ID and select a semester to create a new course.\n          </DialogContentText>\n          \n          <Grid container spacing={2}>\n            <Grid item xs={12}>\n              <TextField\n                autoFocus\n                name=\"course_id\"\n                label=\"Course ID\"\n                placeholder=\"e.g., CS601\"\n                fullWidth\n                value={courseData.course_id}\n                onChange={handleInputChange}\n                margin=\"normal\"\n                required\n                helperText=\"Enter the course ID or name\"\n              />\n            </Grid>\n            \n            <Grid item xs={12}>\n              <FormControl fullWidth margin=\"normal\" required>\n                <InputLabel id=\"semester-select-label\">Semester</InputLabel>\n                <Select\n                  labelId=\"semester-select-label\"\n                  name=\"semester\"\n                  value={courseData.semester}\n                  onChange={handleInputChange}\n                  label=\"Semester\"\n                >\n                  {semesterOptions.map((semester) => (\n                    <MenuItem key={semester} value={semester}>\n                      {semester}\n                    </MenuItem>\n                  ))}\n                </Select>\n              </FormControl>\n            </Grid>\n          </Grid>\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleCreateCourse}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!courseData.course_id || !courseData.semester}\n          >\n            Create\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Delete Course Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete Course\"\n        message={`Are you sure you want to delete the course \"${courseToDelete?.course_id}\" for ${courseToDelete?.semester}? This action cannot be undone.`}\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteCourse}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n          setCourseToDelete(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Course Detail Page (`/src/pages/course/[id]/index.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Course Detail Page for BU MET Autograder\n * Shows course information, instructors, assignments, and course transfer options\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport { useRouter } from 'next/router';\nimport Link from 'next/link';\nimport {\n  Alert,\n  Avatar,\n  AvatarGroup,\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardContent,\n  Chip,\n  Dialog,\n  DialogActions,\n  DialogContent,\n  DialogContentText,\n  DialogTitle,\n  Divider,\n  FormControl,\n  Grid,\n  IconButton,\n  InputLabel,\n  MenuItem,\n  Paper,\n  Select,\n  Snackbar,\n  Tab,\n  Tabs,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  ArrowBack as ArrowBackIcon,\n  Assignment as AssignmentIcon,\n  Description as MaterialsIcon,\n  RuleFolder as RubricsIcon,\n  People as PeopleIcon,\n  Assessment as GradingIcon,\n  SwapHoriz as TransferIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport { courseService, assignmentService, useUser } from '../../../services/api';\nimport CardSkeleton from '../../../components/CardSkeleton';\n\n// Styled components\nconst CourseHeader = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  alignItems: 'center',\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  [theme.breakpoints.down('sm')]: {\n    flexDirection: 'column',\n    alignItems: 'flex-start',\n  },\n}));\n\nconst HeaderTitle = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  flex: 1,\n  [theme.breakpoints.down('sm')]: {\n    width: '100%',\n    marginBottom: theme.spacing(2),\n  },\n}));\n\nconst HeaderActions = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  gap: theme.spacing(1),\n  [theme.breakpoints.down('sm')]: {\n    width: '100%',\n    justifyContent: 'flex-start',\n  },\n}));\n\nconst StyledCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  height: '100%',\n}));\n\nconst TabPanel = (props) => {\n  const { children, value, index, ...other } = props;\n  return (\n    <div\n      role=\"tabpanel\"\n      hidden={value !== index}\n      id={`course-tabpanel-${index}`}\n      aria-labelledby={`course-tab-${index}`}\n      {...other}\n    >\n      {value === index && <Box sx={{ py: 3 }}>{children}</Box>}\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\n// Course detail page component\nexport default function CourseDetail() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  const { id: courseId, semester } = router.query;\n  const { user } = useUser();\n  \n  // State for course data\n  const [course, setCourse] = useState(null);\n  const [assignments, setAssignments] = useState([]);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n  const [error, setError] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for tabs\n  const [tabValue, setTabValue] = useState(0);\n  \n  // State for course transfer dialog\n  const [transferDialogOpen, setTransferDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [transferData, setTransferData] = useState({\n    copyFromCourseId: '',\n    copyFromCourseSemester: '',\n  });\n  const [availableCourses, setAvailableCourses] = useState([]);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Fetch course data and assignments\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchData = async () => {\n      if (!courseId || !semester) return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        // Fetch course details\n        const courseData = await courseService.getCourse(courseId, semester);\n        setCourse(courseData);\n        \n        // Fetch assignments for this course\n        const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(courseId, semester);\n        setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n        \n        // Fetch available courses for transfer\n        const coursesData = await courseService.getCourses();\n        // Filter out current course and only include courses with different semesters\n        const filteredCourses = coursesData.filter(\n          (c) => !(c.course_id === courseId && c.semester === semester)\n        );\n        setAvailableCourses(filteredCourses);\n        \n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching course data:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load course data');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchData();\n  }, [courseId, semester]);\n  \n  // Handle tab change\n  const handleTabChange = (event, newValue) => {\n    setTabValue(newValue);\n  };\n  \n  // Navigate to other course tabs\n  const navigateToTab = (tab) => {\n    router.push(`/course/${courseId}/${tab}?semester=${semester}`);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle course transfer\n  const handleCourseTransfer = async () => {\n    try {\n      await courseService.transferCourse(\n        courseId,\n        semester,\n        transferData.copyFromCourseId,\n        transferData.copyFromCourseSemester\n      );\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setTransferDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Course materials and rubrics transferred successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      \n      // Refresh data\n      const courseData = await courseService.getCourse(courseId, semester);\n      setCourse(courseData);\n      \n      const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(courseId, semester);\n      setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error transferring course:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to transfer course materials');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle form input changes for transfer\n  const handleTransferInputChange = (event) => {\n    const { name, value } = event.target;\n    \n    if (name === 'sourceCourse') {\n      // Parse the combined value (courseId|semester)\n      const [copyFromCourseId, copyFromCourseSemester] = value.split('|');\n      setTransferData({\n        copyFromCourseId,\n        copyFromCourseSemester,\n      });\n    } else {\n      setTransferData({\n        ...transferData,\n        [name]: value,\n      });\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <CourseHeader>\n        <HeaderTitle>\n          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n            <IconButton\n              edge=\"start\"\n              aria-label=\"back to courses\"\n              onClick={() => router.push('/courses')}\n              sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n            >\n              <ArrowBackIcon />\n            </IconButton>\n            \n            <Box>\n              <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n                {loading ? 'Loading...' : course?.course_id}\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                {loading ? 'Loading...' : course?.semester}\n              </Typography>\n            </Box>\n          </Box>\n        </HeaderTitle>\n        \n        <HeaderActions>\n          <Button\n            variant=\"outlined\"\n            startIcon={<TransferIcon />}\n            onClick={() => setTransferDialogOpen(true)}\n          >\n            Transfer Course\n          </Button>\n        </HeaderActions>\n      </CourseHeader>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      <Paper sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n        <Tabs\n          value={tabValue}\n          onChange={handleTabChange}\n          variant=\"scrollable\"\n          scrollButtons=\"auto\"\n          aria-label=\"course tabs\"\n        >\n          <Tab label=\"Overview\" icon={<AssignmentIcon />} iconPosition=\"start\" />\n          <Tab \n            label=\"Assignments\" \n            icon={<AssignmentIcon />} \n            iconPosition=\"start\" \n            onClick={() => navigateToTab('assignments')}\n          />\n          <Tab \n            label=\"Materials\" \n            icon={<MaterialsIcon />} \n            iconPosition=\"start\" \n            onClick={() => navigateToTab('materials')}\n          />\n          <Tab \n            label=\"Rubrics\" \n            icon={<RubricsIcon />} \n            iconPosition=\"start\" \n            onClick={() => navigateToTab('rubrics')}\n          />\n          <Tab \n            label=\"Grading\" \n            icon={<GradingIcon />} \n            iconPosition=\"start\" \n            onClick={() => navigateToTab('grading')}\n          />\n          <Tab \n            label=\"Instructors\" \n            icon={<PeopleIcon />} \n            iconPosition=\"start\" \n            onClick={() => navigateToTab('instructors')}\n          />\n        </Tabs>\n      </Paper>\n      \n      <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={0}>\n        {loading ? (\n          <Grid container spacing={3}>\n            <Grid item xs={12} md={8}>\n              <CardSkeleton height={300} />\n            </Grid>\n            <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n              <CardSkeleton height={300} />\n            </Grid>\n          </Grid>\n        ) : (\n          <Grid container spacing={3}>\n            {/* Course Overview */}\n            <Grid item xs={12} md={8}>\n              <StyledCard>\n                <CardContent>\n                  <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                    Course Overview\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n                  \n                  <Grid container spacing={2}>\n                    <Grid item xs={12} sm={6}>\n                      <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                        Course ID\n                      </Typography>\n                      <Typography variant=\"body1\" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n                        {course?.course_id}\n                      </Typography>\n                    </Grid>\n                    \n                    <Grid item xs={12} sm={6}>\n                      <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                        Semester\n                      </Typography>\n                      <Typography variant=\"body1\" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n                        {course?.semester}\n                      </Typography>\n                    </Grid>\n                    \n                    <Grid item xs={12}>\n                      <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                        Instructors\n                      </Typography>\n                      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 1, mt: 1 }}>\n                        {course?.instructors.map((instructor) => (\n                          <Chip\n                            key={instructor}\n                            label={instructor}\n                            size=\"small\"\n                            avatar={\n                              <Avatar>\n                                {instructor.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}\n                              </Avatar>\n                            }\n                          />\n                        ))}\n                      </Box>\n                    </Grid>\n                  </Grid>\n                  \n                  <Divider sx={{ my: 2 }} />\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                    Assignment Statistics\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Grid container spacing={2}>\n                    <Grid item xs={12} sm={4}>\n                      <Paper\n                        elevation={0}\n                        sx={{\n                          p: 2,\n                          textAlign: 'center',\n                          bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                        }}\n                      >\n                        <Typography variant=\"h5\" color=\"primary\">\n                          {assignments.length}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          Total Assignments\n                        </Typography>\n                      </Paper>\n                    </Grid>\n                    \n                    <Grid item xs={12} sm={4}>\n                      <Paper\n                        elevation={0}\n                        sx={{\n                          p: 2,\n                          textAlign: 'center',\n                          bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                        }}\n                      >\n                        <Typography variant=\"h5\" color=\"primary\">\n                          {/* This would come from a real API call */}\n                          {assignments.reduce((sum, assignment) => sum + (assignment.questions?.length || 0), 0)}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          Total Questions\n                        </Typography>\n                      </Paper>\n                    </Grid>\n                    \n                    <Grid item xs={12} sm={4}>\n                      <Paper\n                        elevation={0}\n                        sx={{\n                          p: 2,\n                          textAlign: 'center',\n                          bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                        }}\n                      >\n                        <Typography variant=\"h5\" color=\"primary\">\n                          {/* This would come from a real API call */}\n                          {course?.instructors.length}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          Instructors\n                        </Typography>\n                      </Paper>\n                    </Grid>\n                  </Grid>\n                </CardContent>\n              </StyledCard>\n            </Grid>\n            \n            {/* Quick Links */}\n            <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n              <StyledCard>\n                <CardContent>\n                  <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                    Quick Links\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n                  \n                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 1 }}>\n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                      fullWidth\n                      startIcon={<AssignmentIcon />}\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}`}\n                    >\n                      Manage Assignments\n                    </Button>\n                    \n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                      fullWidth\n                      startIcon={<MaterialsIcon />}\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/materials?semester=${semester}`}\n                    >\n                      Course Materials\n                    </Button>\n                    \n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                      fullWidth\n                      startIcon={<RubricsIcon />}\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/rubrics?semester=${semester}`}\n                    >\n                      Manage Rubrics\n                    </Button>\n                    \n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                      fullWidth\n                      startIcon={<GradingIcon />}\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/grading?semester=${semester}`}\n                    >\n                      Grade Submissions\n                    </Button>\n                    \n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                      fullWidth\n                      startIcon={<PeopleIcon />}\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/instructors?semester=${semester}`}\n                    >\n                      Manage Instructors\n                    </Button>\n                  </Box>\n                </CardContent>\n              </StyledCard>\n            </Grid>\n            \n            {/* Recent Assignments */}\n            <Grid item xs={12}>\n              <StyledCard>\n                <CardContent>\n                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>\n                    <Typography variant=\"h6\">\n                      Recent Assignments\n                    </Typography>\n                    \n                    <Button\n                      component={Link}\n                      href={`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}`}\n                      size=\"small\"\n                    >\n                      View All\n                    </Button>\n                  </Box>\n                  \n                  <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n                  \n                  {assignments.length === 0 ? (\n                    <Box sx={{ textAlign: 'center', py: 3 }}>\n                      <Typography variant=\"body1\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                        No assignments created yet.\n                      </Typography>\n                      <Button\n                        variant=\"contained\"\n                        component={Link}\n                        href={`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}`}\n                        sx={{ mt: 2 }}\n                      >\n                        Create Assignment\n                      </Button>\n                    </Box>\n                  ) : (\n                    <Grid container spacing={2}>\n                      {assignments.slice(0, 3).map((assignment) => (\n                        <Grid item xs={12} sm={4} key={assignment.assignment_id}>\n                          <Paper\n                            elevation={0}\n                            sx={{\n                              p: 2,\n                              bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                              borderRadius: 2,\n                            }}\n                          >\n                            <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" noWrap>\n                              {assignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n                            </Typography>\n                            <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                              {assignment.questions?.length || 0} questions\n                            </Typography>\n                            <Button\n                              size=\"small\"\n                              component={Link}\n                              href={`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}&assignmentId=${assignment.assignment_id}`}\n                            >\n                              View Details\n                            </Button>\n                          </Paper>\n                        </Grid>\n                      ))}\n                    </Grid>\n                  )}\n                </CardContent>\n              </StyledCard>\n            </Grid>\n          </Grid>\n        )}\n      </TabPanel>\n      \n      {/* Course Transfer Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={transferDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setTransferDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Transfer Course Materials</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <DialogContentText sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n            Select a source course to copy materials, assignments, and rubrics from.\n            This will not affect the source course.\n          </DialogContentText>\n          \n          <FormControl fullWidth margin=\"normal\" required>\n            <InputLabel id=\"source-course-select-label\">Source Course</InputLabel>\n            <Select\n              labelId=\"source-course-select-label\"\n              name=\"sourceCourse\"\n              value={`${transferData.copyFromCourseId}|${transferData.copyFromCourseSemester}`}\n              onChange={handleTransferInputChange}\n              label=\"Source Course\"\n            >\n              {availableCourses.map((course) => (\n                <MenuItem\n                  key={`${course.course_id}-${course.semester}`}\n                  value={`${course.course_id}|${course.semester}`}\n                >\n                  {course.course_id} - {course.semester}\n                </MenuItem>\n              ))}\n            </Select>\n          </FormControl>\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setTransferDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleCourseTransfer}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!transferData.copyFromCourseId || !transferData.copyFromCourseSemester}\n          >\n            Transfer\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Instructor Management Page (`/src/pages/course/[id]/instructors.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Instructor Management Page for BU MET Autograder\n * Allows adding and removing instructors from courses\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport { useRouter } from 'next/router';\nimport {\n  Alert,\n  Avatar,\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardContent,\n  Chip,\n  Divider,\n  IconButton,\n  List,\n  ListItem,\n  ListItemAvatar,\n  ListItemSecondaryAction,\n  ListItemText,\n  Paper,\n  Snackbar,\n  TextField,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  ArrowBack as ArrowBackIcon,\n  Delete as DeleteIcon,\n  Email as EmailIcon,\n  PersonAdd as PersonAddIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport { courseService, useUser } from '../../../services/api';\nimport ConfirmationDialog from '../../../components/ConfirmationDialog';\nimport CardSkeleton from '../../../components/CardSkeleton';\n\n// Styled components\nconst InstructorCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n}));\n\nconst AddInstructorForm = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  alignItems: 'center',\n  gap: theme.spacing(1),\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  [theme.breakpoints.down('sm')]: {\n    flexDirection: 'column',\n    alignItems: 'stretch',\n  },\n}));\n\n// Instructor management page component\nexport default function InstructorManagement() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  const { id: courseId, semester } = router.query;\n  const { user } = useUser();\n  \n  // State for course data\n  const [course, setCourse] = useState(null);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n  const [error, setError] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for instructor management\n  const [newInstructorEmail, setNewInstructorEmail] = useState('');\n  const [instructorToRemove, setInstructorToRemove] = useState(null);\n  const [confirmDialogOpen, setConfirmDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Fetch course data\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchCourse = async () => {\n      if (!courseId || !semester) return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const courseData = await courseService.getCourse(courseId, semester);\n        setCourse(courseData);\n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching course:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load course data');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchCourse();\n  }, [courseId, semester]);\n  \n  // Check if current user is in the instructors list\n  const isCurrentUserInstructor = () => {\n    if (!user || !course) return false;\n    return course.instructors.includes(user.user_email);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle adding a new instructor\n  const handleAddInstructor = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    \n    if (!newInstructorEmail) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await courseService.addInstructor(courseId, semester, newInstructorEmail);\n      \n      // Refresh course data\n      const courseData = await courseService.getCourse(courseId, semester);\n      setCourse(courseData);\n      \n      // Reset form\n      setNewInstructorEmail('');\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Instructor added successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error adding instructor:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to add instructor');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Open confirmation dialog for removing instructor\n  const openRemoveDialog = (instructor) => {\n    setInstructorToRemove(instructor);\n    setConfirmDialogOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle removing an instructor\n  const handleRemoveInstructor = async () => {\n    if (!instructorToRemove) return;\n    \n    // Prevent removing yourself\n    if (user && instructorToRemove === user.user_email) {\n      setAlertMessage('You cannot remove yourself as an instructor');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      setConfirmDialogOpen(false);\n      setInstructorToRemove(null);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    try {\n      await courseService.removeInstructor(courseId, semester, instructorToRemove);\n      \n      // Refresh course data\n      const courseData = await courseService.getCourse(courseId, semester);\n      setCourse(courseData);\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setConfirmDialogOpen(false);\n      setInstructorToRemove(null);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Instructor removed successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error removing instructor:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to remove instructor');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Email validation\n  const isValidEmail = (email) => {\n    // Basic email validation\n    return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(email);\n  };\n  \n  // Generate initials from email\n  const getInitials = (email) => {\n    if (!email) return '';\n    \n    // Try to extract name from email (e.g., john.doe@example.com -> JD)\n    const parts = email.split('@')[0].split('.');\n    if (parts.length >= 2) {\n      return (parts[0].charAt(0) + parts[1].charAt(0)).toUpperCase();\n    }\n    \n    // Fallback to first letter of email\n    return email.charAt(0).toUpperCase();\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <IconButton\n          edge=\"start\"\n          aria-label=\"back to course\"\n          onClick={() => router.push(`/course/${courseId}?semester=${semester}`)}\n          sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n        >\n          <ArrowBackIcon />\n        </IconButton>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Manage Instructors\n        </Typography>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      {loading ? (\n        <CardSkeleton height={400} />\n      ) : (\n        <>\n          <Paper sx={{ p: 3, mb: 3 }}>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              Course Information\n            </Typography>\n            \n            <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n            \n            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 2 }}>\n              <Box sx={{ flexGrow: 1, minWidth: '200px' }}>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                  Course ID\n                </Typography>\n                <Typography variant=\"body1\" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                  {course?.course_id}\n                </Typography>\n              </Box>\n              \n              <Box sx={{ flexGrow: 1, minWidth: '200px' }}>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                  Semester\n                </Typography>\n                <Typography variant=\"body1\" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                  {course?.semester}\n                </Typography>\n              </Box>\n              \n              <Box sx={{ flexGrow: 1, minWidth: '200px' }}>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                  Number of Instructors\n                </Typography>\n                <Typography variant=\"body1\" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                  {course?.instructors.length}\n                </Typography>\n              </Box>\n            </Box>\n          </Paper>\n          \n          <InstructorCard>\n            <CardContent>\n              <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                Add Instructor\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n                Enter the email address of the instructor you want to add to this course.\n                They will have full access to manage assignments, rubrics, and grade submissions.\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <AddInstructorForm component=\"form\" onSubmit={handleAddInstructor}>\n                <TextField\n                  label=\"Instructor Email\"\n                  variant=\"outlined\"\n                  fullWidth\n                  value={newInstructorEmail}\n                  onChange={(e) => setNewInstructorEmail(e.target.value)}\n                  placeholder=\"instructor@example.com\"\n                  error={newInstructorEmail !== '' && !isValidEmail(newInstructorEmail)}\n                  helperText={\n                    newInstructorEmail !== '' && !isValidEmail(newInstructorEmail)\n                      ? 'Please enter a valid email address'\n                      : ''\n                  }\n                  InputProps={{\n                    startAdornment: <EmailIcon color=\"action\" sx={{ mr: 1 }} />,\n                  }}\n                />\n                \n                <Button\n                  variant=\"contained\"\n                  color=\"primary\"\n                  startIcon={<PersonAddIcon />}\n                  type=\"submit\"\n                  disabled={!newInstructorEmail || !isValidEmail(newInstructorEmail)}\n                  sx={{ minWidth: '120px' }}\n                >\n                  Add\n                </Button>\n              </AddInstructorForm>\n            </CardContent>\n          </InstructorCard>\n          \n          <Card>\n            <CardContent>\n              <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                Current Instructors\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Divider sx={{ mb: 2 }} />\n              \n              {course?.instructors.length === 0 ? (\n                <Box sx={{ textAlign: 'center', py: 3 }}>\n                  <Typography variant=\"body1\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                    No instructors assigned to this course yet.\n                  </Typography>\n                </Box>\n              ) : (\n                <List>\n                  {course?.instructors.map((instructor) => {\n                    const isCurrentUser = user && instructor === user.user_email;\n                    \n                    return (\n                      <ListItem\n                        key={instructor}\n                        sx={{\n                          bgcolor: isCurrentUser ? 'action.selected' : 'transparent',\n                          borderRadius: 1,\n                        }}\n                      >\n                        <ListItemAvatar>\n                          <Avatar sx={{ bgcolor: isCurrentUser ? 'primary.main' : 'secondary.main' }}>\n                            {getInitials(instructor)}\n                          </Avatar>\n                        </ListItemAvatar>\n                        \n                        <ListItemText\n                          primary={instructor}\n                          secondary={\n                            isCurrentUser && (\n                              <Chip\n                                label=\"You\"\n                                size=\"small\"\n                                color=\"primary\"\n                                variant=\"outlined\"\n                              />\n                            )\n                          }\n                        />\n                        \n                        <ListItemSecondaryAction>\n                          <IconButton\n                            edge=\"end\"\n                            aria-label=\"delete\"\n                            onClick={() => openRemoveDialog(instructor)}\n                            disabled={course?.instructors.length <= 1}\n                            title={\n                              course?.instructors.length <= 1\n                                ? 'Cannot remove the last instructor'\n                                : 'Remove instructor'\n                            }\n                          >\n                            <DeleteIcon color={course?.instructors.length <= 1 ? 'disabled' : 'error'} />\n                          </IconButton>\n                        </ListItemSecondaryAction>\n                      </ListItem>\n                    );\n                  })}\n                </List>\n              )}\n              \n              {course?.instructors.length <= 1 && (\n                <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                  A course must have at least one instructor. You cannot remove the last instructor.\n                </Alert>\n              )}\n            </CardContent>\n          </Card>\n        </>\n      )}\n      \n      {/* Confirmation Dialog for Removing Instructor */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={confirmDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Remove Instructor\"\n        message={`Are you sure you want to remove ${instructorToRemove} from this course? They will no longer have access to manage assignments, rubrics, or grade submissions.`}\n        confirmText=\"Remove\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleRemoveInstructor}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setConfirmDialogOpen(false);\n          setInstructorToRemove(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 4. ConfirmationDialog Component (`/src/components/ConfirmationDialog.js`)\n\nThis component is used by both the Course List and Instructor Management pages:\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Confirmation Dialog Component for BU MET Autograder\n * Reusable dialog for confirming user actions\n */\n\nimport React from 'react';\nimport {\n  Button,\n  Dialog,\n  DialogActions,\n  DialogContent,\n  DialogContentText,\n  DialogTitle,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Confirmation dialog component\nexport default function ConfirmationDialog({\n  open,\n  title,\n  message,\n  confirmText,\n  cancelText,\n  onConfirm,\n  onCancel,\n  confirmButtonProps = {},\n}) {\n  return (\n    <Dialog\n      open={open}\n      onClose={onCancel}\n      aria-labelledby=\"alert-dialog-title\"\n      aria-describedby=\"alert-dialog-description\"\n      maxWidth=\"sm\"\n      fullWidth\n    >\n      <DialogTitle id=\"alert-dialog-title\">{title}</DialogTitle>\n      <DialogContent>\n        <DialogContentText id=\"alert-dialog-description\">\n          {message}\n        </DialogContentText>\n      </DialogContent>\n      <DialogActions>\n        <Button onClick={onCancel}>{cancelText || 'Cancel'}</Button>\n        <Button\n          onClick={onConfirm}\n          variant=\"contained\"\n          autoFocus\n          {...confirmButtonProps}\n        >\n          {confirmText || 'Confirm'}\n        </Button>\n      </DialogActions>\n    </Dialog>\n  );\n}\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nConfirmationDialog.propTypes = {\n  open: PropTypes.bool.isRequired,\n  title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,\n  message: PropTypes.string.isRequired,\n  confirmText: PropTypes.string,\n  cancelText: PropTypes.string,\n  onConfirm: PropTypes.func.isRequired,\n  onCancel: PropTypes.func.isRequired,\n  confirmButtonProps: PropTypes.object,\n};\n```\n\n### 5. CardSkeleton Component (`/src/components/CardSkeleton.js`)\n\nThis component is used for loading states across multiple pages:\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Card Skeleton Component for BU MET Autograder\n * Displays a loading placeholder for cards and content\n */\n\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Box, Card, Skeleton } from '@mui/material';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Card skeleton component\nexport default function CardSkeleton({ height = 200, variant = 'rectangular', animation = 'pulse' }) {\n  return (\n    <Card sx={{ height: 'auto', width: '100%' }}>\n      <Box sx={{ p: 2 }}>\n        <Skeleton variant=\"text\" width=\"60%\" height={32} animation={animation} />\n        <Skeleton variant=\"text\" width=\"40%\" height={24} animation={animation} />\n        \n        <Box sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n          <Skeleton\n            variant={variant}\n            width=\"100%\"\n            height={height}\n            animation={animation}\n          />\n        </Box>\n        \n        <Box sx={{ mt: 2, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>\n          <Skeleton variant=\"text\" width=\"30%\" height={24} animation={animation} />\n          <Skeleton variant=\"text\" width=\"20%\" height={24} animation={animation} />\n        </Box>\n      </Box>\n    </Card>\n  );\n}\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nCardSkeleton.propTypes = {\n  height: PropTypes.number,\n  variant: PropTypes.oneOf(['text', 'rectangular', 'circular']),\n  animation: PropTypes.oneOf(['pulse', 'wave', false]),\n};\n```\n\nThese components complete the Course Management section of the BU MET Autograder application. They provide:\n\n1. **Course List Page** - A grid view of all courses with creation and deletion functionality\n2. **Course Detail Page** - An overview of course information with tabs for different sections and course transfer capabilities\n3. **Instructor Management Page** - Interface for adding and removing instructors with appropriate safeguards\n4. **Supporting Components** - Reusable confirmation dialog and loading skeleton components\n\nAll these components are responsive, handle error states appropriately, and include proper loading indicators. The course transfer functionality allows instructors to migrate materials between semesters, and the instructor management page prevents removing the last instructor from a course.\n\nLet me know if you'd like any adjustments to these components or if you'd like me to continue with the next stage of implementation!"

Assignments Page (`/src/pages/course/[id]/assignments.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Assignments Page for BU MET Autograder\n * Interface for creating, editing, and managing assignments\n */\n\nimport React, DialogContent,\n  DialogTitle,\n  Divider,\n  Grid,\n  IconButton,\n  List,\n  ListItem,\n  ListItemIcon,\n  ListItemSecondaryAction,\n  ListItemText,\n  Paper,\n  Snackbar,\n  TextField,\n '../../../components/ConfirmationDialog';\n\n// Styled components\nconst AssignmentCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  height: '100%',\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n  transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.2s ease-in-out',\n  '&:hover': {\n    transform: 'translateY(-4px)',\n    boxShadow: theme.shadows[6],\n  },\n}));\n\nconst AssignmentCardContent = styled(CardContent)({\n  flexGrow: 1,\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n});\n\nconst QuestionItem = styled(ListItem)(({ theme, isDragging }) => ({\n  border: `1px solid  boxShadow: isDragging ? theme.shadows[3] : 'none',\n}));\n\nconst NoAssignmentsBox = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  padding: theme.spacing(4),\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.paper,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  marginTop: theme.spacing(4),\n}));\n\n// Main component\nexport default function Assignments() {\n  const router = \n  // State for dialogs\n  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [editAssignmentDialogOpen, setEditAssignmentDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const   assignment_guidelines: '',\n  });\n  \n  const [questionData, setQuestionData] = useState({\n    question_text: '',\n    question_index: 0,\n    question_graphics_figures: null,\n  });\n  \n  const
