const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Fetch assignments\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchAssignments = async () => {\n      if (!courseId || !semester) return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(courseId, semester);\n        setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n        \n        // If an assignment ID is provided in the URL, select it\n        if (selectedAssignmentId) {\n          const assignment = assignmentsData.find(\n            (a) => a.assignment_id === selectedAssignmentId\n          );\n          if (assignment) {\n            setSelectedAssignment(assignment);\n          }\n        }\n        \n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching assignments:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load assignments');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchAssignments();\n  }, [courseId, semester, selectedAssignmentId]);\n  \n  // Handle creating a new assignment\n  const handleCreateAssignment = async () => {\n    try {\n      const newAssignment = await assignmentService.createAssignment({\n        course_id: courseId,\n        semester: semester,\n        assignment_title: newAssignmentData.assignment_title,\n        assignment_guidelines: newAssignmentData.assignment_guidelines,\n        questions: [],\n      });\n      \n      // Add to assignments list\n      setAssignments([...assignments, newAssignment]);\n      \n      // Reset form and close dialog\n      setNewAssignmentData({\n        assignment_title: '',\n        assignment_guidelines: '',\n      });\n      setCreateDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Select the new assignment\n      setSelectedAssignment(newAssignment);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Assignment created successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      \n      // Update URL with new assignment ID\n      router.push(`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}&assignmentId=${newAssignment.assignment_id}`, undefined, { shallow: true });\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error creating assignment:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to create assignment');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle updating an assignment\n  const handleUpdateAssignment = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    try {\n      // Update assignment through the API\n      // This is a simplified version - in a real app, you'd likely have a dedicated update endpoint\n      const updatedAssignment = {\n        ...selectedAssignment,\n        assignment_title: editAssignmentData.assignment_title,\n        assignment_guidelines: editAssignmentData.assignment_guidelines,\n      };\n      \n      // Mock update - in a real implementation, call the API\n      // await assignmentService.updateAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Update in local state\n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.map((assignment) =>\n        assignment.assignment_id === selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n          ? updatedAssignment\n          : assignment\n      );\n      \n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      setSelectedAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setEditAssignmentDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Assignment updated successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error updating assignment:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to update assignment');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle deleting an assignment\n  const handleDeleteAssignment = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await assignmentService.deleteAssignment(selectedAssignment.assignment_id);\n      \n      // Remove from assignments list\n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.filter(\n        (assignment) => assignment.assignment_id !== selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n      );\n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      \n      // Clear selected assignment\n      setSelectedAssignment(null);\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setDeleteAssignmentDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Assignment deleted successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      \n      // Update URL to remove assignmentId\n      router.push(`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}`, undefined, { shallow: true });\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error deleting assignment:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to delete assignment');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle adding a question\n  const handleAddQuestion = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    try {\n      // Determine the next question index\n      const nextIndex = selectedAssignment.questions.length;\n      \n      const newQuestion = {\n        ...questionData,\n        question_index: nextIndex,\n      };\n      \n      await assignmentService.addQuestion({\n        semester: semester,\n        course_id: courseId,\n        assignment_id: selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n        question: newQuestion,\n      });\n      \n      // Update the selected assignment with the new question\n      const updatedQuestions = [...selectedAssignment.questions, newQuestion];\n      const updatedAssignment = {\n        ...selectedAssignment,\n        questions: updatedQuestions,\n      };\n      \n      // Update in local state\n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.map((assignment) =>\n        assignment.assignment_id === selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n          ? updatedAssignment\n          : assignment\n      );\n      \n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      setSelectedAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Reset form and close dialog\n      setQuestionData({\n        question_text: '',\n        question_index: 0,\n        question_graphics_figures: null,\n      });\n      setAddQuestionDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Question added successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error adding question:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to add question');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle editing a question\n  const handleEditQuestion = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await assignmentService.editQuestion({\n        semester: semester,\n        course_id: courseId,\n        assignment_id: selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n        question: questionData,\n      });\n      \n      // Update the selected assignment with the edited question\n      const updatedQuestions = selectedAssignment.questions.map((q) =>\n        q.question_index === questionData.question_index ? questionData : q\n      );\n      \n      const updatedAssignment = {\n        ...selectedAssignment,\n        questions: updatedQuestions,\n      };\n      \n      // Update in local state\n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.map((assignment) =>\n        assignment.assignment_id === selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n          ? updatedAssignment\n          : assignment\n      );\n      \n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      setSelectedAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Reset form and close dialog\n      setQuestionData({\n        question_text: '',\n        question_index: 0,\n        question_graphics_figures: null,\n      });\n      setEditQuestionDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Question updated successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error editing question:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to edit question');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle deleting a question\n  const handleDeleteQuestion = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment || questionToDelete === null) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await assignmentService.removeQuestion(\n        selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n        questionToDelete\n      );\n      \n      // Update the selected assignment by removing the deleted question\n      const updatedQuestions = selectedAssignment.questions.filter(\n        (q) => q.question_index !== questionToDelete\n      );\n      \n      // Reindex remaining questions\n      const reindexedQuestions = updatedQuestions.map((q, index) => ({\n        ...q,\n        question_index: index,\n      }));\n      \n      const updatedAssignment = {\n        ...selectedAssignment,\n        questions: reindexedQuestions,\n      };\n      \n      // Update in local state\n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.map((assignment) =>\n        assignment.assignment_id === selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n          ? updatedAssignment\n          : assignment\n      );\n      \n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      setSelectedAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Close dialog and reset\n      setDeleteQuestionDialogOpen(false);\n      setQuestionToDelete(null);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Question deleted successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error deleting question:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to delete question');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle opening edit assignment dialog\n  const handleOpenEditAssignmentDialog = () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    setEditAssignmentData({\n      assignment_title: selectedAssignment.assignment_title || '',\n      assignment_guidelines: selectedAssignment.assignment_guidelines || '',\n    });\n    \n    setEditAssignmentDialogOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle opening edit question dialog\n  const handleOpenEditQuestionDialog = (question) => {\n    setQuestionData({\n      question_text: question.question_text,\n      question_index: question.question_index,\n      question_graphics_figures: question.question_graphics_figures || null,\n    });\n    \n    setEditQuestionDialogOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle selecting an assignment\n  const handleSelectAssignment = (assignment) => {\n    setSelectedAssignment(assignment);\n    \n    // Update URL with selected assignment ID\n    router.push(`/course/${courseId}/assignments?semester=${semester}&assignmentId=${assignment.assignment_id}`, undefined, { shallow: true });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle drag and drop reordering of questions\n  const handleDragEnd = async (result) => {\n    if (!result.destination || !selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    const { source, destination } = result;\n    \n    // Don't do anything if dropped in the same position\n    if (source.index === destination.index) return;\n    \n    // Reorder the questions array\n    const questions = Array.from(selectedAssignment.questions);\n    const [movedQuestion] = questions.splice(source.index, 1);\n    questions.splice(destination.index, 0, movedQuestion);\n    \n    // Update question indexes to match their new positions\n    const reindexedQuestions = questions.map((q, index) => ({\n      ...q,\n      question_index: index,\n    }));\n    \n    try {\n      // Update the question order via API\n      await assignmentService.modifyQuestionOrder({\n        semester: semester,\n        course_id: courseId,\n        assignment_id: selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n        list_of_question_indexes: reindexedQuestions.map((q) => q.question_index),\n      });\n      \n      // Update local state\n      const updatedAssignment = {\n        ...selectedAssignment,\n        questions: reindexedQuestions,\n      };\n      \n      const updatedAssignments = assignments.map((assignment) =>\n        assignment.assignment_id === selectedAssignment.assignment_id\n          ? updatedAssignment\n          : assignment\n      );\n      \n      setAssignments(updatedAssignments);\n      setSelectedAssignment(updatedAssignment);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Question order updated successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error updating question order:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to update question order');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle form input changes\n  const handleInputChange = (event, formSetter) => {\n    const { name, value } = event.target;\n    formSetter((prev) => ({\n      ...prev,\n      [name]: value,\n    }));\n  };\n  \n  // Render the assignment list\n  const renderAssignmentList = () => {\n    if (loading) {\n      return (\n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          {[1, 2, 3].map((item) => (\n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} key={item}>\n              <CardSkeleton height={150} />\n            </Grid>\n          ))}\n        </Grid>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    if (assignments.length === 0) {\n      return (\n        <NoAssignmentsBox>\n          <AssignmentIcon sx={{ fontSize: 60, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 2 }} />\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n            No Assignments Found\n          </Typography>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" paragraph>\n            You don't have any assignments yet. Create your first assignment to get started.\n          </Typography>\n          <Button\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n            onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}\n          >\n            Create Assignment\n          </Button>\n        </NoAssignmentsBox>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    return (\n      <Grid container spacing={3}>\n        {assignments.map((assignment) => (\n          <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} key={assignment.assignment_id}>\n            <AssignmentCard\n              raised={selectedAssignment?.assignment_id === assignment.assignment_id}\n            >\n              <CardActionArea onClick={() => handleSelectAssignment(assignment)}>\n                <AssignmentCardContent>\n                  <Typography variant=\"h6\" component=\"h2\" noWrap>\n                    {assignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                    {assignment.questions.length} {assignment.questions.length === 1 ? 'question' : 'questions'}\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  {assignment.assignment_guidelines && (\n                    <Typography\n                      variant=\"body2\"\n                      color=\"text.secondary\"\n                      sx={{\n                        overflow: 'hidden',\n                        textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\n                        display: '-webkit-box',\n                        WebkitLineClamp: 2,\n                        WebkitBoxOrient: 'vertical',\n                        mb: 1,\n                      }}\n                    >\n                      {assignment.assignment_guidelines}\n                    </Typography>\n                  )}\n                </AssignmentCardContent>\n              </CardActionArea>\n            </AssignmentCard>\n          </Grid>\n        ))}\n      </Grid>\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Render the selected assignment details\n  const renderAssignmentDetails = () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return null;\n    \n    return (\n      <Box sx={{ mt: 4 }}>\n        <Paper sx={{ p: 3, mb: 3 }}>\n          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'flex-start' }}>\n            <Box>\n              <Typography variant=\"h5\" gutterBottom>\n                {selectedAssignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                {selectedAssignment.questions.length} {selectedAssignment.questions.length === 1 ? 'question' : 'questions'}\n              </Typography>\n            </Box>\n            \n            <Box>\n              <IconButton\n                color=\"primary\"\n                aria-label=\"edit assignment\"\n                onClick={handleOpenEditAssignmentDialog}\n              >\n                <EditIcon />\n              </IconButton>\n              \n              <IconButton\n                color=\"error\"\n                aria-label=\"delete assignment\"\n                onClick={() => setDeleteAssignmentDialogOpen(true)}\n              >\n                <DeleteIcon />\n              </IconButton>\n            </Box>\n          </Box>\n          \n          {selectedAssignment.assignment_guidelines && (\n            <>\n              <Divider sx={{ my: 2 }} />\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                Guidelines:\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n                {selectedAssignment.assignment_guidelines}\n              </Typography>\n            </>\n          )}\n        </Paper>\n        \n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\">Questions</Typography>\n          \n          <Button\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n            onClick={() => setAddQuestionDialogOpen(true)}\n          >\n            Add Question\n          </Button>\n        </Box>\n        \n        {selectedAssignment.questions.length === 0 ? (\n          <Paper sx={{ p: 3, textAlign: 'center' }}>\n            <QuestionIcon sx={{ fontSize: 48, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 2 }} />\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              No Questions Yet\n            </Typography>\n            <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" paragraph>\n              Add questions to this assignment to get started.\n            </Typography>\n            <Button\n              variant=\"contained\"\n              color=\"primary\"\n              startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n              onClick={() => setAddQuestionDialogOpen(true)}\n            >\n              Add Question\n            </Button>\n          </Paper>\n        ) : (\n          <DragDropContext onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}>\n            <Droppable droppableId=\"questions-list\">\n              {(provided) => (\n                <List {...provided.droppableProps} ref={provided.innerRef}>\n                  {selectedAssignment.questions.map((question, index) => (\n                    <Draggable\n                      key={`question-${question.question_index}`}\n                      draggableId={`question-${question.question_index}`}\n                      index={index}\n                    >\n                      {(provided, snapshot) => (\n                        <QuestionItem\n                          ref={provided.innerRef}\n                          {...provided.draggableProps}\n                          isDragging={snapshot.isDragging}\n                        >\n                          <ListItemIcon {...provided.dragHandleProps}>\n                            <DragIndicatorIcon />\n                          </ListItemIcon>\n                          \n                          <ListItemText\n                            primary={`Question ${index + 1}`}\n                            secondary={\n                              <Typography\n                                variant=\"body2\"\n                                color=\"text.secondary\"\n                                sx={{\n                                  overflow: 'hidden',\n                                  textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\n                                  display: '-webkit-box',\n                                  WebkitLineClamp: 2,\n                                  WebkitBoxOrient: 'vertical',\n                                }}\n                              >\n                                {question.question_text}\n                              </Typography>\n                            }\n                          />\n                          \n                          <ListItemSecondaryAction>\n                            <IconButton\n                              edge=\"end\"\n                              aria-label=\"edit\"\n                              onClick={() => handleOpenEditQuestionDialog(question)}\n                              sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n                            >\n                              <EditIcon />\n                            </IconButton>\n                            \n                            <IconButton\n                              edge=\"end\"\n                              aria-label=\"delete\"\n                              onClick={() => {\n                                setQuestionToDelete(question.question_index);\n                                setDeleteQuestionDialogOpen(true);\n                              }}\n                            >\n                              <DeleteIcon />\n                            </IconButton>\n                          </ListItemSecondaryAction>\n                        </QuestionItem>\n                      )}\n                    </Draggable>\n                  ))}\n                  {provided.placeholder}\n                </List>\n              )}\n            </Droppable>\n          </DragDropContext>\n        )}\n      </Box>\n    );\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <IconButton\n          edge=\"start\"\n          aria-label=\"back to course\"\n          onClick={() => router.push(`/course/${courseId}?semester=${semester}`)}\n          sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n        >\n          <ArrowBackIcon />\n        </IconButton>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Assignments\n        </Typography>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <Typography variant=\"h5\">\n          {selectedAssignment ? 'All Assignments' : 'Course Assignments'}\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <Button\n          variant=\"contained\"\n          color=\"primary\"\n          startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n          onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(true)}\n        >\n          Create Assignment\n        </Button>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {renderAssignmentList()}\n      \n      {renderAssignmentDetails()}\n      \n      {/* Create Assignment Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={createDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setCreateDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Create New Assignment</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            name=\"assignment_title\"\n            label=\"Assignment Title\"\n            fullWidth\n            value={newAssignmentData.assignment_title}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setNewAssignmentData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n          />\n          \n          <TextField\n            name=\"assignment_guidelines\"\n            label=\"Assignment Guidelines\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={4}\n            value={newAssignmentData.assignment_guidelines}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setNewAssignmentData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            helperText=\"Include any general instructions or requirements for the assignment\"\n          />\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setCreateDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleCreateAssignment}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!newAssignmentData.assignment_title}\n          >\n            Create\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Edit Assignment Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={editAssignmentDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setEditAssignmentDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Edit Assignment</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            name=\"assignment_title\"\n            label=\"Assignment Title\"\n            fullWidth\n            value={editAssignmentData.assignment_title}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setEditAssignmentData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n          />\n          \n          <TextField\n            name=\"assignment_guidelines\"\n            label=\"Assignment Guidelines\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={4}\n            value={editAssignmentData.assignment_guidelines}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setEditAssignmentData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            helperText=\"Include any general instructions or requirements for the assignment\"\n          />\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setEditAssignmentDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleUpdateAssignment}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!editAssignmentData.assignment_title}\n          >\n            Update\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Add Question Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={addQuestionDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setAddQuestionDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Add Question</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            name=\"question_text\"\n            label=\"Question Text\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={4}\n            value={questionData.question_text}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setQuestionData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n            helperText=\"Enter the text of the question\"\n          />\n          \n          {/* In a real implementation, add graphics/figures upload here */}\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setAddQuestionDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleAddQuestion}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!questionData.question_text}\n          >\n            Add Question\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Edit Question Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={editQuestionDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setEditQuestionDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Edit Question</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            name=\"question_text\"\n            label=\"Question Text\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={4}\n            value={questionData.question_text}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setQuestionData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n            helperText=\"Enter the text of the question\"\n          />\n          \n          {/* In a real implementation, add graphics/figures upload here */}\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setEditQuestionDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleEditQuestion}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!questionData.question_text}\n          >\n            Update Question\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Delete Assignment Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteAssignmentDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete Assignment\"\n        message={`Are you sure you want to delete \"${selectedAssignment?.assignment_title || 'this assignment'}\"? This action cannot be undone and will remove all associated questions and rubrics.`}\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteAssignment}\n        onCancel={() => setDeleteAssignmentDialogOpen(false)}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Delete Question Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteQuestionDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete Question\"\n        message=\"Are you sure you want to delete this question? This action cannot be undone.\"\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteQuestion}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setDeleteQuestionDialogOpen(false);\n          setQuestionToDelete(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Course Materials Page (`/src/pages/course/[id]/materials.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Course Materials Page for BU MET Autograder\n * Handles file uploads, updates, and deletions\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { useRouter } from 'next/router';\nimport {\n  Alert,\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardActions,\n  CardContent,\n  Chip,\n  Dialog,\n  DialogActions,\n  DialogContent,\n  DialogTitle,\n  Divider,\n  Grid,\n  IconButton,\n  LinearProgress,\n  Link,\n  Paper,\n  Snackbar,\n  TextField,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  ArrowBack as ArrowBackIcon,\n  AttachFile as AttachFileIcon,\n  Delete as DeleteIcon,\n  Edit as EditIcon,\n  FilePresent as FileIcon,\n  PictureAsPdf as PdfIcon,\n  Description as DocIcon,\n  Slideshow as SlideIcon,\n  Code as CodeIcon,\n  Archive as ZipIcon,\n  InsertDriveFile as GenericFileIcon,\n  CloudUpload as UploadIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport { useDropzone } from 'react-dropzone';\nimport { courseService, materialService } from '../../../services/api';\nimport CardSkeleton from '../../../components/CardSkeleton';\nimport ConfirmationDialog from '../../../components/ConfirmationDialog';\nimport { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/config';\n\n// Styled components\nconst MaterialCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  height: '100%',\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n  transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.2s ease-in-out',\n  '&:hover': {\n    transform: 'translateY(-4px)',\n    boxShadow: theme.shadows[6],\n  },\n}));\n\nconst MaterialCardContent = styled(CardContent)({\n  flexGrow: 1,\n});\n\nconst MaterialCardActions = styled(CardActions)(({ theme }) => ({\n  justifyContent: 'space-between',\n  borderTop: `1px solid ${theme.palette.divider}`,\n}));\n\nconst FileIconWrapper = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  justifyContent: 'center',\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(2),\n}));\n\nconst DropzoneContainer = styled(Box)(({ theme, isDragActive, isDragAccept, isDragReject }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n  alignItems: 'center',\n  justifyContent: 'center',\n  padding: theme.spacing(4),\n  borderWidth: 2,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  borderColor: isDragAccept\n    ? theme.palette.success.main\n    : isDragReject\n    ? theme.palette.error.main\n    : isDragActive\n    ? theme.palette.primary.main\n    : theme.palette.divider,\n  borderStyle: 'dashed',\n  backgroundColor: isDragActive\n    ? theme.palette.action.hover\n    : theme.palette.background.default,\n  color: theme.palette.text.primary,\n  outline: 'none',\n  transition: 'border .24s ease-in-out',\n  cursor: 'pointer',\n}));\n\nconst NoMaterialsBox = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  padding: theme.spacing(4),\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.paper,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  marginTop: theme.spacing(4),\n}));\n\n// Main component\nexport default function CourseMaterials() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  const { id: courseId, semester } = router.query;\n  \n  // State for materials\n  const [materials, setMaterials] = useState([]);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n  const [error, setError] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for upload\n  const [uploadDialogOpen, setUploadDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [uploadProgress, setUploadProgress] = useState(0);\n  const [isUploading, setIsUploading] = useState(false);\n  const [uploadFile, setUploadFile] = useState(null);\n  const [uploadFormData, setUploadFormData] = useState({\n    material_name: '',\n    additional_notes: '',\n  });\n  \n  // State for edit\n  const [editDialogOpen, setEditDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [editMaterial, setEditMaterial] = useState(null);\n  const [editFormData, setEditFormData] = useState({\n    material_name: '',\n    additional_notes: '',\n  });\n  \n  // State for delete\n  const [deleteDialogOpen, setDeleteDialogOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [materialToDelete, setMaterialToDelete] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Fetch materials\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchMaterials = async () => {\n      if (!courseId || !semester) return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const materialsData = await materialService.getMaterials(courseId, semester);\n        setMaterials(materialsData || []);\n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching materials:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load course materials');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchMaterials();\n  }, [courseId, semester]);\n  \n  // File upload handlers\n  const onDrop = useCallback((acceptedFiles) => {\n    if (acceptedFiles.length === 0) return;\n    \n    const file = acceptedFiles[0];\n    \n    // Check file size\n    if (file.size > APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize) {\n      setAlertMessage(`File size exceeds the maximum limit of ${APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize / (1024 * 1024)}MB`);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Check file type\n    const fileExtension = `.${file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase()}`;\n    if (!APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.materials.includes(fileExtension)) {\n      setAlertMessage(`File type not supported. Accepted types: ${APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.materials.join(', ')}`);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    setUploadFile(file);\n    setUploadFormData({\n      ...uploadFormData,\n      material_name: file.name,\n    });\n    \n    setUploadDialogOpen(true);\n  }, [uploadFormData]);\n  \n  const { getRootProps, getInputProps, isDragActive, isDragAccept, isDragReject } = useDropzone({\n    onDrop,\n    accept: {\n      'application/pdf': ['.pdf'],\n      'application/msword': ['.doc'],\n      'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document': ['.docx'],\n      'application/vnd.ms-powerpoint': ['.ppt'],\n      'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation': ['.pptx'],\n      'text/plain': ['.txt'],\n      'application/zip': ['.zip'],\n    },\n    multiple: false,\n  });\n  \n  // Handle uploading a material\n  const handleUploadMaterial = async () => {\n    if (!uploadFile || !uploadFormData.material_name) return;\n    \n    setIsUploading(true);\n    setUploadProgress(0);\n    \n    try {\n      // Read file as base64\n      const reader = new FileReader();\n      \n      reader.onloadstart = () => {\n        setUploadProgress(0);\n      };\n      \n      reader.onprogress = (event) => {\n        if (event.lengthComputable) {\n          const progress = Math.round((event.loaded / event.total) * 100);\n          setUploadProgress(progress);\n        }\n      };\n      \n      reader.onload = async () => {\n        const base64Data = reader.result.split(',')[1]; // Remove the data URL prefix\n        \n        // Create material data object\n        const materialData = {\n          course_id: courseId,\n          semester: semester,\n          material_id: `${Date.now()}-${uploadFile.name.replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}`, // Generate a unique ID\n          material_name: uploadFormData.material_name,\n          additional_notes: uploadFormData.additional_notes || null,\n          data: {\n            data_type: `.${uploadFile.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase()}`,\n            content: base64Data,\n            metadata: {\n              size: `${uploadFile.size}`,\n              type: uploadFile.type,\n              name: uploadFile.name,\n            },\n          },\n        };\n        \n        // Upload material\n        const result = await materialService.uploadMaterial(materialData);\n        \n        // Add to materials list\n        setMaterials([...materials, result]);\n        \n        // Reset form and close dialog\n        setUploadFile(null);\n        setUploadFormData({\n          material_name: '',\n          additional_notes: '',\n        });\n        setUploadDialogOpen(false);\n        setIsUploading(false);\n        \n        // Show success alert\n        setAlertMessage('Material uploaded successfully');\n        setAlertSeverity('success');\n        setAlertOpen(true);\n      };\n      \n      reader.onerror = () => {\n        throw new Error('Error reading file');\n      };\n      \n      reader.readAsDataURL(uploadFile);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error uploading material:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to upload material');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      setIsUploading(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle updating a material\n  const handleUpdateMaterial = async () => {\n    if (!editMaterial) return;\n    \n    try {\n      const updatedMaterial = {\n        ...editMaterial,\n        material_name: editFormData.material_name,\n        additional_notes: editFormData.additional_notes || null,\n      };\n      \n      await materialService.updateMaterial(updatedMaterial);\n      \n      // Update materials list\n      const updatedMaterials = materials.map((material) =>\n        material.material_id === editMaterial.material_id ? updatedMaterial : material\n      );\n      setMaterials(updatedMaterials);\n      \n      // Reset form and close dialog\n      setEditMaterial(null);\n      setEditFormData({\n        material_name: '',\n        additional_notes: '',\n      });\n      setEditDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Material updated successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error updating material:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to update material');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle deleting a material\n  const handleDeleteMaterial = async () => {\n    if (!materialToDelete) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await materialService.deleteMaterial(\n        courseId,\n        semester,\n        materialToDelete.material_id\n      );\n      \n      // Remove from materials list\n      const updatedMaterials = materials.filter(\n        (material) => material.material_id !== materialToDelete.material_id\n      );\n      setMaterials(updatedMaterials);\n      \n      // Close dialog\n      setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n      setMaterialToDelete(null);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Material deleted successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error deleting material:', error);\n      setAlertMessage(error.message || 'Failed to delete material');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle opening edit dialog\n  const handleOpenEditDialog = (material) => {\n    setEditMaterial(material);\n    setEditFormData({\n      material_name: material.material_name,\n      additional_notes: material.additional_notes || '',\n    });\n    setEditDialogOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle form input changes\n  const handleInputChange = (event, formSetter) => {\n    const { name, value } = event.target;\n    formSetter((prev) => ({\n      ...prev,\n      [name]: value,\n    }));\n  };\n  \n  // Get file icon based on file type\n  const getFileIcon = (fileType) => {\n    if (!fileType) return <GenericFileIcon fontSize=\"large\" />;\n    \n    switch (fileType.toLowerCase()) {\n      case '.pdf':\n        return <PdfIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"error\" />;\n      case '.doc':\n      case '.docx':\n        return <DocIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"primary\" />;\n      case '.ppt':\n      case '.pptx':\n        return <SlideIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"warning\" />;\n      case '.txt':\n        return <FileIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"info\" />;\n      case '.zip':\n        return <ZipIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"action\" />;\n      default:\n        return <GenericFileIcon fontSize=\"large\" />;\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <IconButton\n          edge=\"start\"\n          aria-label=\"back to course\"\n          onClick={() => router.push(`/course/${courseId}?semester=${semester}`)}\n          sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n        >\n          <ArrowBackIcon />\n        </IconButton>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Course Materials\n        </Typography>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      <Paper sx={{ p: 3, mb: 4 }}>\n        <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n          Upload New Materials\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n          Drag and drop files here or click to browse. Supported file types: PDF, DOC, DOCX, PPT, PPTX, TXT, ZIP.\n          Maximum file size: {APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize / (1024 * 1024)}MB.\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <DropzoneContainer\n          {...getRootProps()}\n          isDragActive={isDragActive}\n          isDragAccept={isDragAccept}\n          isDragReject={isDragReject}\n        >\n          <input {...getInputProps()} />\n          \n          <UploadIcon sx={{ fontSize: 48, mb: 2, color: 'action.active' }} />\n          \n          {isDragActive ? (\n            <Typography variant=\"body1\">Drop the file here...</Typography>\n          ) : (\n            <Typography variant=\"body1\">\n              Drag and drop a file here, or click to select a file\n            </Typography>\n          )}\n          \n          <Button\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            startIcon={<AttachFileIcon />}\n            sx={{ mt: 2 }}\n          >\n            Browse Files\n          </Button>\n        </DropzoneContainer>\n      </Paper>\n      \n      <Typography variant=\"h5\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n        All Materials\n      </Typography>\n      \n      {loading ? (\n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((item) => (\n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={item}>\n              <CardSkeleton height={180} />\n            </Grid>\n          ))}\n        </Grid>\n      ) : materials.length === 0 ? (\n        <NoMaterialsBox>\n          <FileIcon sx={{ fontSize: 60, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 2 }} />\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n            No Materials Found\n          </Typography>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" paragraph>\n            You haven't uploaded any course materials yet. Upload your first material to get started.\n          </Typography>\n          <Button\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            startIcon={<UploadIcon />}\n            onClick={() => {\n              // Trigger the file input click\n              document.querySelector('input[type=\"file\"]').click();\n            }}\n          >\n            Upload Material\n          </Button>\n        </NoMaterialsBox>\n      ) : (\n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          {materials.map((material) => (\n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={material.material_id}>\n              <MaterialCard>\n                <MaterialCardContent>\n                  <FileIconWrapper>\n                    {getFileIcon(material.data.data_type)}\n                  </FileIconWrapper>\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"h6\" component=\"h2\" align=\"center\" noWrap gutterBottom>\n                    {material.material_name}\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Box sx={{ mb: 1 }}>\n                    <Chip\n                      label={material.data.data_type.replace('.', '').toUpperCase()}\n                      size=\"small\"\n                      color={\n                        material.data.data_type === '.pdf' ? 'error' :\n                        material.data.data_type === '.doc' || material.data.data_type === '.docx' ? 'primary' :\n                        material.data.data_type === '.ppt' || material.data.data_type === '.pptx' ? 'warning' :\n                        'default'\n                      }\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                    />\n                  </Box>\n                  \n                  {material.additional_notes && (\n                    <Typography\n                      variant=\"body2\"\n                      color=\"text.secondary\"\n                      sx={{\n                        overflow: 'hidden',\n                        textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\n                        display: '-webkit-box',\n                        WebkitLineClamp: 2,\n                        WebkitBoxOrient: 'vertical',\n                        mt: 1,\n                      }}\n                    >\n                      {material.additional_notes}\n                    </Typography>\n                  )}\n                </MaterialCardContent>\n                \n                <MaterialCardActions>\n                  <Button\n                    size=\"small\"\n                    component={Link}\n                    href={material.data.url || '#'}\n                    target=\"_blank\"\n                    rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"\n                  >\n                <IconButton\n                      size=\"small\"\n                      color=\"error\"\n                      onClick={() => {\n          </IconButton>\n                  </Box>\n                </MaterialCardActions>\n              </MaterialCard>\n            </Grid>\n          ))}\n        </Grid>\n      )}\n      \n      {/* Upload Material Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={uploadDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => !isUploading && setUploadDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Upload Material</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          {isUploading && (\n            <Box sx={{ width: '100%', mb: 2 }}>\n              <LinearProgress            </Typography>\n            </Box>\n          )}\n          \n          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>\n        name=\"additional_notes\"\n            label=\"Additional Notes\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={3}\n            value={uploadFormData.additional_notes}\n disabled={!uploadFormData.material_name || isUploading}\n            startIcon={<UploadIcon />}\n          >\n            {isUploading ? {editMaterial?.data.data_type}\n            </Typography>\n          </Box>\n          \n          <TextField\n            name=\"material_name\"\n            label=\"Material Name\"\n            fullWidth\n            value={editFormData.material_name}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setEditFormData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n          />\n value={editFormData.additional_notes}\n            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, setEditFormData)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            helperText=\"Optional notes about this onClick={handleUpdateMaterial}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!editFormData.material_name}\n          >\n            Update\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Delete Material Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete Material\"\n        message={`Are you sure you want to delete \"${materialToDelete?.material_name}\"? This action cannot be undone.`}\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteMaterial}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n          setMaterialToDelete(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\nThese components implement the Assignments and Materials management features for the BU MET Autograder. They provide:\n\n1. **Assignments Page** - A comprehensive interface for:\n   - Creating and managing assignments\n   - Adding, editing, and deleting questions\n   - Reordering questions with drag-and-drop functionality\n   - Viewing assignment details and guidelines\n\n2. **Course Materials Page** - A robust file management system with:\n   - Drag-and-drop file uploads with progress indication\n   - File type validation and size limits\n   - Material editing and deletion\n   - Organized display of different file types with appropriate icons\n\nBoth pages include proper error handling, loading states, and responsive design to ensure a smooth user experience across different devices. Switch,\n  Tab,\n  Tabs,\n  TextField,\n  Tooltip,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  Add as AddIcon,\n  ArrowBack as ArrowBackIcon,\n return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(courseId, semester);\n        setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n        \n        // If an assignment ID is provided in the URL, select it\n        if (selectedAssignmentId) {\n          const assignment = assignmentsData.find(\n            (a) => a.assignment_id ===    }\n        \n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching assignments:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load assignments');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchAssignments();\n  }, [courseId, semester, selectedAssignmentId]);\n  \n  // Fetch rubric for selected assignment\n  const fetchRubric = async (assignmentId) => {\n    try {\n      const rubricData = await rubricService.getRubric(assignmentId);\n      setRubric(rubricData);\n      \n      // Set default current question rubricData;\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error fetching rubric:', err);\n      // If no rubric exists, create an empty one\n      const emptyRubric = createEmptyRubric(assignmentId);\n      setRubric(emptyRubric);\n      return emptyRubric;\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Create an empty rubric structure\n  const createEmptyRubric = (assignmentId) => {\n    const assignment =
