    grading_flags: [],\n      leniency: 3, // Default leniency (1-5)\n      overall_instructor_guidelines: '',\n      sub_rubrics: subRubrics,\n    };\n  };\n  \n  // Handle selecting an assignment\n  const handleSelectAssignment = async (assignment) => {\n    setSelectedAssignment(assignment);\n    setTabValue(0); // Reset to the first tab\n    \n    // Fetch or create rubric for this assignment\n    await fetchRubric(assignment.assignment_id);\n    \n    // Update URL with selected assignment ID\n    router.push(`/course/${courseId}/rubrics?semester=${semester}&assignmentId=${assignment.assignment_id}`, undefined, { shallow: true });\n  };\n  \n  // Get AI-generated rubric suggestions\n  const getAIRubricSuggestions = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    setLoadingAI(true);\n    try {\n      const aiRubricData = await rubricService.getAIRubric(\n        selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n        aiInstructions || null\n      );\n      \n      setAiRubric(aiRubricData);\n      setAiInstructionsDialogOpen(false);\n      setAiInstructions('');\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('AI-generated rubric suggestions received');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error getting AI rubric suggestions:', err);\n      setAlertMessage(err.message || 'Failed to get AI rubric suggestions');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } finally {\n      setLoadingAI(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Apply AI rubric suggestions to current rubric\n  const applyAIRubricSuggestions = () => {\n    if (!aiRubric) return;\n    \n    setRubric(aiRubric);\n    setAiRubric(null);\n    \n    // Show success alert\n    setAlertMessage('AI rubric suggestions applied');\n    setAlertSeverity('success');\n    setAlertOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Save rubric changes\n  const saveRubric = async () => {\n    if (!rubric) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await rubricService.createRubric(rubric);\n      \n      setEditMode(false);\n      \n      // Show success alert\n      setAlertMessage('Rubric saved successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving rubric:', err);\n      setAlertMessage(err.message || 'Failed to save rubric');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle adding a grading criteria\n  const handleAddCriteria = () => {\n    if (!rubric || !selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    // Find the current sub-rubric\n    const currentSubRubric = rubric.sub_rubrics.find(\n      (sr) => sr.question_index === currentQuestionIndex\n    );\n    \n    if (!currentSubRubric) return;\n    \n    // Add the new criteria\n    const newCriteria = {\n      criteria_id: criteriaData.criteria_id,\n      criteria: criteriaData.criteria,\n      points: parseFloat(criteriaData.points),\n    };\n    \n    // Update the sub-rubric's grading criteria\n    const updatedSubRubrics = rubric.sub_rubrics.map((sr) => {\n      if (sr.question_index === currentQuestionIndex) {\n        return {\n          ...sr,\n          grading_criteria: [...(sr.grading_criteria || []), newCriteria],\n        };\n      }\n      return sr;\n    });\n    \n    // Update the rubric\n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      sub_rubrics: updatedSubRubrics,\n    });\n    \n    // Reset form and close dialog\n    setCriteriaData({\n      criteria_id: '',\n      criteria: '',\n      points: 0,\n    });\n    setCriteriaDialogOpen(false);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle editing a grading criteria\n  const handleEditCriteria = (subRubricIndex, criteriaIndex, updatedCriteria) => {\n    if (!rubric) return;\n    \n    // Create a deep copy of the sub_rubrics array\n    const updatedSubRubrics = [...rubric.sub_rubrics];\n    \n    // Update the specific criteria\n    if (updatedSubRubrics[subRubricIndex].grading_criteria) {\n      updatedSubRubrics[subRubricIndex].grading_criteria[criteriaIndex] = updatedCriteria;\n    }\n    \n    // Update the rubric\n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      sub_rubrics: updatedSubRubrics,\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle deleting a grading criteria\n  const handleDeleteCriteria = () => {\n    if (!rubric || !criteriaToDelete) return;\n    \n    const { subRubricIndex, criteriaIndex } = criteriaToDelete;\n    \n    // Create a deep copy of the sub_rubrics array\n    const updatedSubRubrics = [...rubric.sub_rubrics];\n    \n    // Remove the criteria\n    if (updatedSubRubrics[subRubricIndex].grading_criteria) {\n      updatedSubRubrics[subRubricIndex].grading_criteria.splice(criteriaIndex, 1);\n    }\n    \n    // Update the rubric\n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      sub_rubrics: updatedSubRubrics,\n    });\n    \n    // Close dialog\n    setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n    setCriteriaToDelete(null);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle updating overall rubric settings\n  const handleRubricSettingChange = (field, value) => {\n    if (!rubric) return;\n    \n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      [field]: value,\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle updating sub-rubric settings\n  const handleSubRubricChange = (questionIndex, field, value) => {\n    if (!rubric) return;\n    \n    const updatedSubRubrics = rubric.sub_rubrics.map((sr) => {\n      if (sr.question_index === questionIndex) {\n        return {\n          ...sr,\n          [field]: value,\n        };\n      }\n      return sr;\n    });\n    \n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      sub_rubrics: updatedSubRubrics,\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle toggling grading flags\n  const handleGradingFlagToggle = (flag) => {\n    if (!rubric) return;\n    \n    const currentFlags = rubric.grading_flags || [];\n    const updatedFlags = currentFlags.includes(flag)\n      ? currentFlags.filter((f) => f !== flag)\n      : [...currentFlags, flag];\n    \n    setRubric({\n      ...rubric,\n      grading_flags: updatedFlags,\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle tab change\n  const handleTabChange = (event, newValue) => {\n    setTabValue(newValue);\n  };\n  \n  // Get the question text for a given index\n  const getQuestionText = (questionIndex) => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return '';\n    \n    const question = selectedAssignment.questions.find(\n      (q) => q.question_index === questionIndex\n    );\n    \n    return question ? question.question_text : '';\n  };\n  \n  // Calculate total points for a sub-rubric\n  const calculateTotalPoints = (subRubric) => {\n    if (!subRubric || !subRubric.grading_criteria) return 0;\n    \n    return subRubric.grading_criteria.reduce(\n      (sum, criteria) => sum + parseFloat(criteria.points),\n      0\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Render assignment selection section\n  const renderAssignmentSelection = () => {\n    if (loading) {\n      return <CardSkeleton height={100} />;\n    }\n    \n    if (assignments.length === 0) {\n      return (\n        <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          No assignments found. Create an assignment first to define rubrics.\n        </Alert>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    return (\n      <Grid container spacing={3} sx={{ mb: 4 }}>\n        {assignments.map((assignment) => (\n          <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} key={assignment.assignment_id}>\n            <StyledCard\n              raised={selectedAssignment?.assignment_id === assignment.assignment_id}\n              onClick={() => handleSelectAssignment(assignment)}\n              sx={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}\n            >\n              <CardContent>\n                <Typography variant=\"h6\" component=\"h2\" noWrap>\n                  {assignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n                </Typography>\n                \n                <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                  {assignment.questions.length} {assignment.questions.length === 1 ? 'question' : 'questions'}\n                </Typography>\n                \n                <Chip\n                  label={selectedAssignment?.assignment_id === assignment.assignment_id ? 'Selected' : 'Select'}\n                  color={selectedAssignment?.assignment_id === assignment.assignment_id ? 'primary' : 'default'}\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  sx={{ mt: 1 }}\n                />\n              </CardContent>\n            </StyledCard>\n          </Grid>\n        ))}\n      </Grid>\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Render rubric tabs and content\n  const renderRubricContent = () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment || !rubric) return null;\n    \n    return (\n      <>\n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>\n          <Typography variant=\"h5\">\n            Rubric for {selectedAssignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n          </Typography>\n          \n          <Box>\n            {editMode ? (\n              <>\n                <Button\n                  variant=\"contained\"\n                  color=\"primary\"\n                  startIcon={<SaveIcon />}\n                  onClick={saveRubric}\n                  sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n                >\n                  Save\n                </Button>\n                <Button\n                  variant=\"outlined\"\n                  onClick={() => setEditMode(false)}\n                >\n                  Cancel\n                </Button>\n              </>\n            ) : (\n              <>\n                <Button\n                  variant=\"outlined\"\n                  startIcon={<LightbulbIcon />}\n                  onClick={() => setAiInstructionsDialogOpen(true)}\n                  sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n                >\n                  Get AI Suggestions\n                </Button>\n                <Button\n                  variant=\"contained\"\n                  startIcon={<EditIcon />}\n                  onClick={() => setEditMode(true)}\n                >\n                  Edit Rubric\n                </Button>\n              </>\n            )}\n          </Box>\n        </Box>\n        \n        <Paper sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          <Tabs\n            value={tabValue}\n            onChange={handleTabChange}\n            variant=\"scrollable\"\n            scrollButtons=\"auto\"\n            aria-label=\"rubric tabs\"\n          >\n            <Tab label=\"Overall Guidelines\" />\n            {rubric.sub_rubrics.map((subRubric) => (\n              <Tab\n                key={`question-${subRubric.question_index}`}\n                label={`Question ${subRubric.question_index + 1}`}\n                onClick={() => setCurrentQuestionIndex(subRubric.question_index)}\n              />\n            ))}\n          </Tabs>\n        </Paper>\n        \n        {/* Overall Guidelines Tab */}\n        <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={0}>\n          <RubricSection>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              General Rubric Settings\n            </Typography>\n            \n            <Grid container spacing={3}>\n              <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>\n                <TextField\n                  label=\"Overall Instructor Guidelines\"\n                  multiline\n                  rows={4}\n                  fullWidth\n                  value={rubric.overall_instructor_guidelines || ''}\n                  onChange={(e) => handleRubricSettingChange('overall_instructor_guidelines', e.target.value)}\n                  disabled={!editMode}\n                  placeholder=\"Enter general grading instructions applicable to all questions\"\n                  variant=\"outlined\"\n                  margin=\"normal\"\n                />\n              </Grid>\n              \n              <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                  Leniency Level\n                </Typography>\n                \n                <Box sx={{ px: 2 }}>\n                  <Slider\n                    value={rubric.leniency || 3}\n                    min={1}\n                    max={5}\n                    step={1}\n                    marks={[\n                      { value: 1, label: 'Strict' },\n                      { value: 2, label: '' },\n                      { value: 3, label: 'Moderate' },\n                      { value: 4, label: '' },\n                      { value: 5, label: 'Lenient' },\n                    ]}\n                    valueLabelDisplay=\"auto\"\n                    onChange={(e, value) => handleRubricSettingChange('leniency', value)}\n                    disabled={!editMode}\n                  />\n                </Box>\n                \n                <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                  Leniency determines how strictly the responses will be graded. Higher leniency allows for more flexibility in answers.\n                </Typography>\n              </Grid>\n              \n              <Grid item xs={12}>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                  Grading Flags\n                </Typography>\n                \n                <FormGroup row>\n                  {gradingFlags.map((flag) => (\n                    <Tooltip key={flag.value} title={flag.description} arrow>\n                      <FormControlLabel\n                        control={\n                          <Switch\n                            checked={(rubric.grading_flags || []).includes(flag.value)}\n                            onChange={() => handleGradingFlagToggle(flag.value)}\n                            disabled={!editMode}\n                            color=\"primary\"\n                          />\n                        }\n                        label={flag.label}\n                      />\n                    </Tooltip>\n                  ))}\n                </FormGroup>\n              </Grid>\n            </Grid>\n          </RubricSection>\n        </TabPanel>\n        \n        {/* Question-specific Sub-rubric Tabs */}\n        {rubric.sub_rubrics.map((subRubric, subRubricIndex) => (\n          <TabPanel\n            key={`subRubric-${subRubric.question_index}`}\n            value={tabValue}\n            index={subRubricIndex + 1}\n          >\n            <RubricSection>\n              <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                Question {subRubric.question_index + 1}\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Typography\n                variant=\"body1\"\n                sx={{\n                  bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                  p: 2,\n                  borderRadius: 1,\n                  mb: 3,\n                }}\n              >\n                {getQuestionText(subRubric.question_index)}\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Grid container spacing={3}>\n                <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>\n                  <TextField\n                    label=\"Instructor Guideline\"\n                    multiline\n                    rows={4}\n                    fullWidth\n                    value={subRubric.instructor_guideline || ''}\n                    onChange={(e) =>\n                      handleSubRubricChange(\n                        subRubric.question_index,\n                        'instructor_guideline',\n                        e.target.value\n                      )\n                    }\n                    disabled={!editMode}\n                    placeholder=\"Enter specific instructions for grading this question\"\n                    variant=\"outlined\"\n                    margin=\"normal\"\n                  />\n                </Grid>\n                \n                <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>\n                  <TextField\n                    label=\"Maximum Points\"\n                    type=\"number\"\n                    fullWidth\n                    value={subRubric.max_points || 0}\n                    onChange={(e) =>\n                      handleSubRubricChange(\n                        subRubric.question_index,\n                        'max_points',\n                        parseFloat(e.target.value)\n                      )\n                    }\n                    disabled={!editMode}\n                    InputProps={{\n                      inputProps: { min: 0, step: 0.5 },\n                    }}\n                    variant=\"outlined\"\n                    margin=\"normal\"\n                  />\n                  \n                  <FormControl fullWidth margin=\"normal\">\n                    <InputLabel id={`leniency-select-${subRubric.question_index}`}>\n                      Question-specific Leniency\n                    </InputLabel>\n                    <Select\n                      labelId={`leniency-select-${subRubric.question_index}`}\n                      value={subRubric.leniency || ''}\n                      onChange={(e) =>\n                        handleSubRubricChange(\n                          subRubric.question_index,\n                          'leniency',\n                          e.target.value === '' ? null : parseInt(e.target.value)\n                        )\n                      }\n                      disabled={!editMode}\n                      label=\"Question-specific Leniency\"\n                    >\n                      <MenuItem value=\"\">\n                        <em>Use global leniency</em>\n                      </MenuItem>\n                      <MenuItem value={1}>1 - Very Strict</MenuItem>\n                      <MenuItem value={2}>2 - Strict</MenuItem>\n                      <MenuItem value={3}>3 - Moderate</MenuItem>\n                      <MenuItem value={4}>4 - Lenient</MenuItem>\n                      <MenuItem value={5}>5 - Very Lenient</MenuItem>\n                    </Select>\n                  </FormControl>\n                </Grid>\n              </Grid>\n            </RubricSection>\n            \n            <RubricSection>\n              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>\n                <Typography variant=\"h6\">\n                  Grading Criteria\n                </Typography>\n                \n                {editMode && (\n                  <Button\n                    variant=\"contained\"\n                    color=\"primary\"\n                    startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n                    onClick={() => setCriteriaDialogOpen(true)}\n                  >\n                    Add Criteria\n                  </Button>\n                )}\n              </Box>\n              \n              {(!subRubric.grading_criteria || subRubric.grading_criteria.length === 0) ? (\n                <Box sx={{ textAlign: 'center', py: 3 }}>\n                  <RubricIcon sx={{ fontSize: 48, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 1 }} />\n                  <Typography variant=\"body1\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                    No grading criteria defined yet.\n                  </Typography>\n                  {editMode && (\n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"contained\"\n                      color=\"primary\"\n                      startIcon={<AddIcon />}\n                      onClick={() => setCriteriaDialogOpen(true)}\n                      sx={{ mt: 2 }}\n                    >\n                      Add Criteria\n                    </Button>\n                  )}\n                </Box>\n              ) : (\n                <>\n                  {subRubric.grading_criteria.map((criteria, criteriaIndex) => (\n                    <CriteriaCard key={`criteria-${criteriaIndex}`}>\n                      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'flex-start' }}>\n                        <Box>\n                          <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" fontWeight=\"bold\">\n                            {criteria.criteria_id || `Criteria ${criteriaIndex + 1}`}\n                          </Typography>\n                          \n                          <Typography variant=\"body2\" sx={{ mt: 1 }}>\n                            {criteria.criteria}\n                          </Typography>\n                        </Box>\n                        \n                        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n                          <Chip\n                            label={`${criteria.points} points`}\n                            color=\"primary\"\n                            variant=\"outlined\"\n                          />\n                          \n                          {editMode && (\n                            <IconButton\n                              color=\"error\"\n                              size=\"small\"\n                              onClick={() => {\n                                setCriteriaToDelete({\n                                  subRubricIndex,\n                                  criteriaIndex,\n                                });\n                                setDeleteDialogOpen(true);\n                              }}\n                              sx={{ ml: 1 }}\n                            >\n                              <DeleteIcon fontSize=\"small\" />\n                            </IconButton>\n                          )}\n                        </Box>\n                      </Box>\n                    </CriteriaCard>\n                  ))}\n                  \n                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', mt: 2 }}>\n                    <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\">\n                      Total Points: {calculateTotalPoints(subRubric)}\n                    </Typography>\n                    \n                    <Typography\n                      variant=\"subtitle1\"\n                      color={\n                        calculateTotalPoints(subRubric) === parseFloat(subRubric.max_points)\n                          ? 'success.main'\n                          : 'error.main'\n                      }\n                    >\n                      {calculateTotalPoints(subRubric) === parseFloat(subRubric.max_points)\n                        ? 'Points match maximum'\n                        : `Warning: Total (${calculateTotalPoints(subRubric)}) doesn't match maximum (${subRubric.max_points})`}\n                    </Typography>\n                  </Box>\n                </>\n              )}\n            </RubricSection>\n          </TabPanel>\n        ))}\n      </>\n    );\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <IconButton\n          edge=\"start\"\n          aria-label=\"back to course\"\n          onClick={() => router.push(`/course/${courseId}?semester=${semester}`)}\n          sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n        >\n          <ArrowBackIcon />\n        </IconButton>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Rubric Management\n        </Typography>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      <Typography variant=\"h5\" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n        Select an Assignment\n      </Typography>\n      \n      {renderAssignmentSelection()}\n      \n      {renderRubricContent()}\n      \n      {/* AI Suggestion Card */}\n      {aiRubric && (\n        <AISuggestionCard\n          rubric={aiRubric}\n          onApply={applyAIRubricSuggestions}\n          onDismiss={() => setAiRubric(null)}\n        />\n      )}\n      \n      {/* Add Criteria Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={criteriaDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setCriteriaDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Add Grading Criteria</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            label=\"Criteria Title\"\n            fullWidth\n            value={criteriaData.criteria_id}\n            onChange={(e) => setCriteriaData({ ...criteriaData, criteria_id: e.target.value })}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n            placeholder=\"e.g., Correct Logic, Proper Format, etc.\"\n          />\n          \n          <TextField\n            label=\"Criteria Description\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={3}\n            value={criteriaData.criteria}\n            onChange={(e) => setCriteriaData({ ...criteriaData, criteria: e.target.value })}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n            placeholder=\"Describe what constitutes fulfilling this criteria\"\n          />\n          \n          <TextField\n            label=\"Points\"\n            type=\"number\"\n            fullWidth\n            value={criteriaData.points}\n            onChange={(e) => setCriteriaData({ ...criteriaData, points: e.target.value })}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            required\n            InputProps={{\n              inputProps: { min: 0, step: 0.5 },\n              endAdornment: <InputAdornment position=\"end\">points</InputAdornment>,\n            }}\n          />\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setCriteriaDialogOpen(false)}>Cancel</Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleAddCriteria}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!criteriaData.criteria_id || !criteriaData.criteria || criteriaData.points <= 0}\n          >\n            Add\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Delete Criteria Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete Grading Criteria\"\n        message=\"Are you sure you want to delete this grading criteria? This action cannot be undone.\"\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteCriteria}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n          setCriteriaToDelete(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* AI Instructions Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={aiInstructionsDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => !loadingAI && setAiInstructionsDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>\n          <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n            <LightbulbIcon sx={{ mr: 1, color: 'warning.main' }} />\n            AI Rubric Suggestions\n          </Box>\n        </DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n            Our AI can analyze your assignment and questions to suggest a comprehensive rubric.\n            You can provide specific instructions to guide the AI.\n          </Typography>\n          \n          <TextField\n            label=\"Instructions for AI (Optional)\"\n            fullWidth\n            multiline\n            rows={4}\n            value={aiInstructions}\n            onChange={(e) => setAiInstructions(e.target.value)}\n            margin=\"normal\"\n            placeholder=\"e.g., Focus on logical reasoning, prioritize code efficiency, etc.\"\n            disabled={loadingAI}\n          />\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button\n            onClick={() => setAiInstructionsDialogOpen(false)}\n            disabled={loadingAI}\n          >\n            Cancel\n          </Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={getAIRubricSuggestions}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={loadingAI}\n            startIcon={loadingAI ? null : <LightbulbIcon />}\n          >\n            {loadingAI ? 'Generating...' : 'Get AI Suggestions'}\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Grading Dashboard (`/src/pages/course/[id]/grading.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Grading Dashboard for BU MET Autograder\n * Displays student submissions for grading and review\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport { useRouter } from 'next/router';\nimport {\n  Alert,\n  Badge,\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardContent,\n  Chip,\n  CircularProgress,\n  Divider,\n  FormControl,\n  Grid,\n  IconButton,\n  InputLabel,\n  MenuItem,\n  Paper,\n  Select,\n  Snackbar,\n  Tab,\n  Tabs,\n  TextField,\n  Tooltip,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  ArrowBack as ArrowBackIcon,\n  Assignment as AssignmentIcon,\n  AssignmentTurnedIn as GradedIcon,\n  Assessment as GradeIcon,\n  Refresh as RefreshIcon,\n  Search as SearchIcon,\n  FilterList as FilterIcon,\n  PersonSearch as StudentSearchIcon,\n  QuestionAnswer as QuestionIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport { assignmentService, responseService } from '../../../services/api';\nimport CardSkeleton from '../../../components/CardSkeleton';\nimport GradingModeSelect from '../../../components/GradingModeSelect';\nimport SelectableList from '../../../components/SelectableList';\nimport ConfirmationDialog from '../../../components/ConfirmationDialog';\n\n// Styled components\nconst StyledCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  height: '100%',\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n}));\n\nconst GradingActionCard = styled(Paper)(({ theme }) => ({\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n}));\n\nconst ResponseCard = styled(Paper)(({ theme }) => ({\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  borderLeft: `4px solid ${theme.palette.primary.main}`,\n}));\n\nconst GradeCard = styled(Paper)(({ theme, gradePercent }) => ({\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  borderLeft: `4px solid ${\n    gradePercent >= 90\n      ? theme.palette.custom.gradeA\n      : gradePercent >= 80\n      ? theme.palette.custom.gradeB\n      : gradePercent >= 70\n      ? theme.palette.custom.gradeC\n      : gradePercent >= 60\n      ? theme.palette.custom.gradeD\n      : theme.palette.custom.gradeF\n  }`,\n}));\n\nconst TabPanel = (props) => {\n  const { children, value, index, ...other } = props;\n  return (\n    <div\n      role=\"tabpanel\"\n      hidden={value !== index}\n      id={`grading-tabpanel-${index}`}\n      aria-labelledby={`grading-tab-${index}`}\n      {...other}\n    >\n      {value === index && <Box sx={{ pt: 3 }}>{children}</Box>}\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\n// Main component\nexport default function GradingDashboard() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  const { id: courseId, semester } = router.query;\n  \n  // State for assignments and submissions\n  const [assignments, setAssignments] = useState([]);\n  const [selectedAssignment, setSelectedAssignment] = useState(null);\n  const [responses, setResponses] = useState([]);\n  const [filteredResponses, setFilteredResponses] = useState([]);\n  const [selectedResponse, setSelectedResponse] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for loading and error\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);\n  const [loadingResponses, setLoadingResponses] = useState(false);\n  const [grading, setGrading] = useState(false);\n  const [error, setError] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for filters and search\n  const [questionFilter, setQuestionFilter] = useState('all');\n  const [gradingStatusFilter, setGradingStatusFilter] = useState('all');\n  const [studentSearch, setStudentSearch] = useState('');\n  \n  // State for grading\n  const [gradingMode, setGradingMode] = useState('ungraded');\n  const [selectedStudents, setSelectedStudents] = useState([]);\n  const [confirmGradingOpen, setConfirmGradingOpen] = useState(false);\n  \n  // State for tabs\n  const [tabValue, setTabValue] = useState(0);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Fetch assignments\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchAssignments = async () => {\n      if (!courseId || !semester) return;\n      \n      setLoading(true);\n      try {\n        const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(courseId, semester);\n        setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n        \n        // If there are assignments, select the first one by default\n        if (assignmentsData && assignmentsData.length > 0) {\n          setSelectedAssignment(assignmentsData[0]);\n          await fetchResponses(assignmentsData[0].assignment_id);\n        }\n        \n        setError(null);\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error fetching assignments:', err);\n        setError(err.message || 'Failed to load assignments');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchAssignments();\n  }, [courseId, semester]);\n  \n  // Fetch responses for selected assignment\n  const fetchResponses = async (assignmentId, questionIndex = null) => {\n    setLoadingResponses(true);\n    try {\n      const responsesData = await responseService.getResponses(assignmentId, questionIndex);\n      setResponses(responsesData || []);\n      setFilteredResponses(responsesData || []);\n      setSelectedResponse(null);\n      setSelectedStudents([]);\n      return responsesData;\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error fetching responses:', err);\n      setAlertMessage(err.message || 'Failed to load responses');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n      return [];\n    } finally {\n      setLoadingResponses(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle selecting an assignment\n  const handleSelectAssignment = async (assignment) => {\n    setSelectedAssignment(assignment);\n    setQuestionFilter('all');\n    setGradingStatusFilter('all');\n    setStudentSearch('');\n    await fetchResponses(assignment.assignment_id);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle selecting a response\n  const handleSelectResponse = (response) => {\n    setSelectedResponse(response);\n    setTabValue(0); // Switch to the response tab\n  };\n  \n  // Apply filters to responses\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!responses) return;\n    \n    let filtered = [...responses];\n    \n    // Filter by question\n    if (questionFilter !== 'all') {\n      filtered = filtered.filter(\n        (response) => response.question_index === parseInt(questionFilter)\n      );\n    }\n    \n    // Filter by grading status\n    if (gradingStatusFilter === 'graded') {\n      filtered = filtered.filter((response) => response.grade);\n    } else if (gradingStatusFilter === 'ungraded') {\n      filtered = filtered.filter((response) => !response.grade);\n    }\n    \n    // Filter by student search\n    if (studentSearch) {\n      filtered = filtered.filter((response) =>\n        response.student_id.toLowerCase().includes(studentSearch.toLowerCase())\n      );\n    }\n    \n    setFilteredResponses(filtered);\n  }, [responses, questionFilter, gradingStatusFilter, studentSearch]);\n  \n  // Handle starting the grading process\n  const handleStartGrading = () => {\n    setConfirmGradingOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle the actual grading process\n  const handleGradeSubmissions = async () => {\n    setConfirmGradingOpen(false);\n    setGrading(true);\n    \n    try {\n      let gradedResponses;\n      const questionIndexToGrade = questionFilter === 'all' ? null : parseInt(questionFilter);\n      \n      switch (gradingMode) {\n        case 'specific':\n          // Grade specific students\n          if (selectedStudents.length === 0) {\n            throw new Error('No students selected for grading');\n          }\n          \n          gradedResponses = await responseService.gradeSpecific(\n            selectedStudents,\n            selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n            questionIndexToGrade\n          );\n          break;\n          \n        case 'ungraded':\n          // Grade all ungraded responses\n          gradedResponses = await responseService.gradeUngraded(\n            selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n            questionIndexToGrade\n          );\n          break;\n          \n        case 'all':\n          // Grade/regrade all responses\n          gradedResponses = await responseService.gradeAll(\n            selectedAssignment.assignment_id,\n            questionIndexToGrade\n          );\n          break;\n          \n        default:\n          throw new Error('Invalid grading mode');\n      }\n      \n      // Refresh responses after grading\n      await fetchResponses(selectedAssignment.assignment_id, questionIndexToGrade);\n      \n      // Show success message\n      setAlertMessage(\n        `Successfully graded ${gradedResponses.length} ${\n          gradedResponses.length === 1 ? 'response' : 'responses'\n        }`\n      );\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error grading submissions:', err);\n      setAlertMessage(err.message || 'Failed to grade submissions');\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } finally {\n      setGrading(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle refreshing responses\n  const handleRefreshResponses = async () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return;\n    \n    const questionIndexToFetch = questionFilter === 'all' ? null : parseInt(questionFilter);\n    await fetchResponses(selectedAssignment.assignment_id, questionIndexToFetch);\n    \n    setAlertMessage('Responses refreshed');\n    setAlertSeverity('success');\n    setAlertOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle tab change\n  const handleTabChange = (event, newValue) => {\n    setTabValue(newValue);\n  };\n  \n  // Calculate grade percentage\n  const calculateGradePercentage = (points, maxPoints) => {\n    if (!points || !maxPoints) return 0;\n    return (points / maxPoints) * 100;\n  };\n  \n  // Get letter grade based on percentage\n  const getLetterGrade = (percentage) => {\n    if (percentage >= 90) return 'A';\n    if (percentage >= 80) return 'B';\n    if (percentage >= 70) return 'C';\n    if (percentage >= 60) return 'D';\n    return 'F';\n  };\n  \n  // Count ungraded responses\n  const countUngradedResponses = () => {\n    return responses.filter((response) => !response.grade).length;\n  };\n  \n  // Count responses for a specific question\n  const countResponsesForQuestion = (questionIndex) => {\n    return responses.filter((response) => response.question_index === questionIndex).length;\n  };\n  \n  // Count ungraded responses for a specific question\n  const countUngradedResponsesForQuestion = (questionIndex) => {\n    return responses.filter(\n      (response) => response.question_index === questionIndex && !response.grade\n    ).length;\n  };\n  \n  // Render assignment selection section\n  const renderAssignmentSelection = () => {\n    if (loading) {\n      return <CardSkeleton height={100} />;\n    }\n    \n    if (assignments.length === 0) {\n      return (\n        <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          No assignments found. Create an assignment first to grade submissions.\n        </Alert>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    return (\n      <FormControl fullWidth variant=\"outlined\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n        <InputLabel id=\"assignment-select-label\">Assignment</InputLabel>\n        <Select\n          labelId=\"assignment-select-label\"\n          value={selectedAssignment?.assignment_id || ''}\n          onChange={(e) => {\n            const assignment = assignments.find((a) => a.assignment_id === e.target.value);\n            if (assignment) {\n              handleSelectAssignment(assignment);\n            }\n          }}\n          label=\"Assignment\"\n        >\n          {assignments.map((assignment) => (\n            <MenuItem key={assignment.assignment_id} value={assignment.assignment_id}>\n              {assignment.assignment_title || 'Untitled Assignment'}\n            </MenuItem>\n          ))}\n        </Select>\n      </FormControl>\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Render grading actions section\n  const renderGradingActions = () => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return null;\n    \n    return (\n      <GradingActionCard>\n        <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n          Grading Actions\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <Grid container spacing={3}>\n          <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n            <GradingModeSelect\n              value={gradingMode}\n              onChange={setGradingMode}\n              disabled={grading}\n            />\n          </Grid>\n          \n          <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n            <FormControl fullWidth variant=\"outlined\">\n              <InputLabel id=\"question-filter-label\">Question</InputLabel>\n              <Select\n                labelId=\"question-filter-label\"\n                value={questionFilter}\n                onChange={(e) => setQuestionFilter(e.target.value)}\n                label=\"Question\"\n                disabled={grading}\n              >\n                <MenuItem value=\"all\">All Questions</MenuItem>\n                {selectedAssignment.questions.map((question) => (\n                  <MenuItem key={question.question_index} value={question.question_index}>\n                    Question {question.question_index + 1}{' '}\n                    <Badge\n                      badgeContent={countUngradedResponsesForQuestion(question.question_index)}\n                      color=\"error\"\n                      sx={{ ml: 1 }}\n                    />\n                  </MenuItem>\n                ))}\n              </Select>\n            </FormControl>\n          </Grid>\n          \n          <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1 }}>\n              <Button\n                variant=\"contained\"\n                color=\"primary\"\n                fullWidth\n                onClick={handleStartGrading}\n                disabled={\n                  grading ||\n                  responses.length === 0 ||\n                  (gradingMode === 'ungraded' && countUngradedResponses() === 0) ||\n                  (gradingMode === 'specific' && selectedStudents.length === 0)\n                }\n                startIcon={<GradeIcon />}\n              >\n                {grading ? 'Grading...' : 'Start Grading'}\n              </Button>\n              \n              <Tooltip title=\"Refresh Responses\">\n                <IconButton\n                  color=\"primary\"\n                  onClick={handleRefreshResponses}\n                  disabled={grading || loadingResponses}\n                >\n                  <RefreshIcon />\n                </IconButton>\n              </Tooltip>\n            </Box>\n          </Grid>\n          \n          <Grid item xs={12}>\n            <Divider sx={{ my: 1 }} />\n            \n            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 2 }}>\n              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n                <FilterIcon sx={{ mr: 1, color: 'action.active' }} />\n                <FormControl variant=\"outlined\" size=\"small\" sx={{ minWidth: 150 }}>\n                  <InputLabel id=\"status-filter-label\">Status</InputLabel>\n                  <Select\n                    labelId=\"status-filter-label\"\n                    value={gradingStatusFilter}\n                    onChange={(e) => setGradingStatusFilter(e.target.value)}\n                    label=\"Status\"\n                    disabled={grading}\n                  >\n                    <MenuItem value=\"all\">All Responses</MenuItem>\n                    <MenuItem value=\"graded\">Graded Only</MenuItem>\n                    <MenuItem value=\"ungraded\">Ungraded Only</MenuItem>\n                  </Select>\n                </FormControl>\n              </Box>\n              \n              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexGrow: 1 }}>\n                <StudentSearchIcon sx={{ mr: 1, color: 'action.active' }} />\n                <TextField\n                  label=\"Search Student\"\n                  variant=\"outlined\"\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  fullWidth\n                  value={studentSearch}\n                  onChange={(e) => setStudentSearch(e.target.value)}\n                  disabled={grading}\n                  InputProps={{\n                    endAdornment: studentSearch ? (\n                      <IconButton\n                        size=\"small\"\n                        onClick={() => setStudentSearch('')}\n                        edge=\"end\"\n                      >\n                        <SearchIcon />\n                      </IconButton>\n                    ) : null,\n                  }}\n                />\n              </Box>\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                {filteredResponses.length} {filteredResponses.length === 1 ? 'response' : 'responses'} •{' '}\n                {countUngradedResponses()} ungraded\n              </Typography>\n            </Box>\n          </Grid>\n        </Grid>\n      </GradingActionCard>\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Render responses list and details\n  const renderResponsesContent = () => {\n    if (loadingResponses) {\n      return (\n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', my: 4 }}>\n          <CircularProgress />\n        </Box>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    if (filteredResponses.length === 0) {\n      return (\n        <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n          No responses found matching the current filters.\n        </Alert>\n      );\n    }\n    \n    return (\n      <Grid container spacing={3}>\n        <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n            Student Responses\n          </Typography>\n          \n          <SelectableList\n            items={filteredResponses}\n            keyField=\"student_id\"\n            secondaryKeyField=\"question_index\"\n            selectedItems={selectedStudents}\n            onSelectionChange={setSelectedStudents}\n            onItemClick={handleSelectResponse}\n            highlightedItem={selectedResponse}\n            selectionMode={gradingMode === 'specific' ? 'multiple' : 'none'}\n            renderItem={(response) => (\n              <Box>\n                <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" noWrap>\n                  {response.student_id}\n                </Typography>\n                <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                  Question {response.question_index + 1}\n                </Typography>\n                <Box sx={{ mt: 1, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>\n                  {response.grade ? (\n                    <>\n                      <GradedIcon\n                        fontSize=\"small\"\n                        color=\"success\"\n                        sx={{ mr: 0.5 }}\n                      />\n                      <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"success.main\">\n                        Graded: {response.grade.points}/{response.grade.max_points} points\n                      </Typography>\n                    </>\n                  ) : (\n                    <Chip\n                      label=\"Ungraded\"\n                      size=\"small\"\n                      color=\"warning\"\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                    />\n                  )}\n                </Box>\n              </Box>\n            )}\n          />\n        </Grid>\n        \n        <Grid item xs={12} md={8}>\n          {selectedResponse ? (\n            <>\n              <Paper sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n                <Tabs\n                  value={tabValue}\n                  onChange={handleTabChange}\n                  variant=\"fullWidth\"\n                  aria-label=\"response tabs\"\n                >\n                  <Tab label=\"Response\" icon={<QuestionIcon />} iconPosition=\"start\" />\n                  <Tab\n                    label=\"Grade\"\n                    icon={<GradedIcon />}\n                    iconPosition=\"start\"\n                    disabled={!selectedResponse.grade}\n                  />\n                </Tabs>\n              </Paper>\n              \n              <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={0}>\n                <ResponseCard>\n                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', mb: 2 }}>\n                    <Typography variant=\"h6\">\n                      {selectedResponse.student_id}\n                    </Typography>\n                    \n                    <Chip\n                      label={selectedResponse.grade ? 'Graded' : 'Ungraded'}\n                      color={selectedResponse.grade ? 'success' : 'warning'}\n                      variant=\"outlined\"\n                    />\n                  </Box>\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                    Question {selectedResponse.question_index + 1}:\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n                    {getQuestionText(selectedResponse.question_index)}\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Divider sx={{ mb: 3 }} />\n                  \n                  <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                    Student Response:\n                  </Typography>\n                  \n                  <Paper\n                    elevation={0}\n                    sx={{\n                      p: 2,\n                      bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                      borderRadius: 1,\n                      whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap',\n                    }}\n                  >\n                    {/* \n                      In a real implementation, this would render the response data\n                      based on its type (text, file, etc.)\n                    */}\n                    {selectedResponse.data.content || 'No response content available'}\n                  </Paper>\n                </ResponseCard>\n              </TabPanel>\n              \n              <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={1}>\n                {selectedResponse.grade ? (\n                  <GradeCard\n                    gradePercent={calculateGradePercentage(\n                      selectedResponse.grade.points,\n                      selectedResponse.grade.max_points\n                    )}\n                  >\n                    <Box\n                      sx={{\n                        display: 'flex',\n                        justifyContent: 'space-between',\n                        alignItems: 'flex-start',\n                        mb: 2,\n                      }}\n                    >\n                      <Typography variant=\"h6\">\n                        Grade for {selectedResponse.student_id}\n                      </Typography>\n                      \n                      <Box sx={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>\n                        <Typography variant=\"h4\" color=\"primary\">\n                          {selectedResponse.grade.points}/{selectedResponse.grade.max_points}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          {calculateGradePercentage(\n                            selectedResponse.grade.points,\n                            selectedResponse.grade.max_points\n                          ).toFixed(1)}\n                          % ({getLetterGrade(\n                            calculateGradePercentage(\n                              selectedResponse.grade.points,\n                              selectedResponse.grade.max_points\n                            )\n                          )})\n                        </Typography>\n                      </Box>\n                    </Box>\n                    \n                    <Divider sx={{ mb: 3 }} />\n                    \n                    <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                      Grading Explanation:\n                    </Typography>\n                    \n                    <Paper\n                      elevation={0}\n                      sx={{\n                        p: 2,\n                        bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                        borderRadius: 1,\n                        whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap',\n                      }}\n                    >\n                      {selectedResponse.grade.explanation || 'No explanation provided'}\n                    </Paper>\n                  </GradeCard>\n                ) : (\n                  <Alert severity=\"info\">\n                    This response has not been graded yet.\n                  </Alert>\n                )}\n              </TabPanel>\n            </>\n          ) : (\n            <Paper\n              sx={{\n                p: 3,\n                display: 'flex',\n                flexDirection: 'column',\n                alignItems: 'center',\n                justifyContent: 'center',\n                height: 300,\n              }}\n            >\n              <AssignmentIcon sx={{ fontSize: 48, color: 'text.secondary', mb: 2 }} />\n              <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n                No Response Selected\n              </Typography>\n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" align=\"center\">\n                Select a student response from the list to view details and grading information.\n              </Typography>\n            </Paper>\n          )}\n        </Grid>\n      </Grid>\n    );\n  };\n  \n  // Helper function to get question text\n  const getQuestionText = (questionIndex) => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) return '';\n    \n    const question = selectedAssignment.questions.find(\n      (q) => q.question_index === questionIndex\n    );\n    \n    return question ? question.question_text : '';\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 3 }}>\n        <IconButton\n          edge=\"start\"\n          aria-label=\"back to course\"\n          onClick={() => router.push(`/course/${courseId}?semester=${semester}`)}\n          sx={{ mr: 1 }}\n        >\n          <ArrowBackIcon />\n        </IconButton>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\">\n          Grading Dashboard\n        </Typography>\n      </Box>\n      \n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n      \n      {renderAssignmentSelection()}\n      \n      {selectedAssignment && renderGradingActions()}\n      \n      {selectedAssignment && renderResponsesContent()}\n      \n      {/* Grading Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={confirmGradingOpen}\n        title=\"Confirm Grading Action\"\n        message={\n          gradingMode === 'specific'\n            ? `You are about to grade ${selectedStudents.length} selected student ${\n                selectedStudents.length === 1 ? 'response' : 'responses'\n              }. This process may take some time. Do you want to continue?`\n            : gradingMode === 'ungraded'\n            ? `You are about to grade all ungraded responses${\n                questionFilter !== 'all'\n                  ? ` for Question ${parseInt(questionFilter) + 1}`\n                  : ''\n              }. This process may take some time. Do you want to continue?`\n            : `You are about to grade/regrade ALL responses${\n                questionFilter !== 'all'\n                  ? ` for Question ${parseInt(questionFilter) + 1}`\n                  : ''\n              }. This will overwrite any existing grades. This process may take some time. Do you want to continue?`\n        }\n        confirmText=\"Start Grading\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        onConfirm={handleGradeSubmissions}\n        onCancel={() => setConfirmGradingOpen(false)}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </Box>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 3. AI Suggestion Card Component (`/src/components/AISuggestionCard.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * AI Suggestion Card Component for BU MET Autograder\n * Displays AI-generated rubric suggestions\n */\n\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport {\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardActions,\n  CardContent,\n  Collapse,\n  Divider,\n  IconButton,\n  List,\n  ListItem,\n  ListItemIcon,\n  ListItemText,\n  Paper,\n  Tooltip,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  Check as CheckIcon,\n  Close as CloseIcon,\n  ExpandMore as ExpandMoreIcon,\n  Lightbulb as LightbulbIcon,\n  RuleFolder as RubricIcon,\n  Assignment as CriteriaIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Styled components\nconst SuggestionCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  position: 'relative',\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.mode === 'dark' \n    ? theme.palette.background.paper \n    : theme.palette.common.white,\n  boxShadow: theme.shadows[4],\n  borderLeft: `4px solid ${theme.palette.warning.main}`,\n}));\n\nconst ExpandButton = styled(IconButton)(({ theme, expanded }) => ({\n  transform: expanded ? 'rotate(180deg)' : 'rotate(0deg)',\n  transition: theme.transitions.create('transform', {\n    duration: theme.transitions.duration.shortest,\n  }),\n}));\n\nconst CriteriaItem = styled(ListItem)(({ theme }) => ({\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.default,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(1),\n}));\n\n// AI Suggestion Card component\nconst AISuggestionCard = ({ rubric, onApply, onDismiss }) => {\n  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);\n  \n  // Toggle expanded state\n  const handleExpandClick = () => {\n    setExpanded(!expanded);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle applying the suggestion\n  const handleApply = () => {\n    if (onApply) onApply(rubric);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle dismissing the suggestion\n  const handleDismiss = () => {\n    if (onDismiss) onDismiss();\n  };\n  \n  return (\n    <SuggestionCard>\n      <CardContent>\n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 1 }}>\n          <LightbulbIcon sx={{ color: 'warning.main', mr: 1 }} />\n          <Typography variant=\"h6\">\n            AI-Generated Rubric Suggestion\n          </Typography>\n        </Box>\n        \n        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n          Our AI has analyzed your assignment and generated a suggested rubric. Review the suggestion and apply it if you find it useful.\n        </Typography>\n        \n        <Paper\n          elevation={0}\n          sx={{ bgcolor: 'background.default', p: 2, borderRadius: 1 }}\n        >\n          <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n            <RubricIcon fontSize=\"small\" sx={{ mr: 1, verticalAlign: 'middle' }} />\n            Overall Guidelines\n          </Typography>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n            {rubric.overall_instructor_guidelines || 'No overall guidelines provided.'}\n          </Typography>\n        </Paper>\n        \n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mt: 2 }}>\n          <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\">\n            {rubric.sub_rubrics.length} Questions\n          </Typography>\n          \n          <ExpandButton\n            expanded={expanded}\n            onClick={handleExpandClick}\n            aria-expanded={expanded}\n            aria-label=\"show more\"\n            size=\"small\"\n          >\n            <ExpandMoreIcon />\n          </ExpandButton>\n        </Box>\n      </CardContent>\n      \n      <Collapse in={expanded} timeout=\"auto\" unmountOnExit>\n        <CardContent sx={{ pt: 0 }}>\n          <Divider sx={{ my: 2 }} />\n          \n          {rubric.sub_rubrics.map((subRubric, index) => (\n            <Box key={`subRubric-${index}`} sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n              <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                Question {subRubric.question_index + 1} - {subRubric.max_points} points\n              </Typography>\n              \n              <Typography variant=\"body2\" paragraph>\n                {subRubric.instructor_guideline || 'No specific guidelines for this question.'}\n              </Typography>\n              \n              {subRubric.grading_criteria && subRubric.grading_criteria.length > 0 && (\n                <List dense disablePadding>\n                  {subRubric.grading_criteria.map((criteria, criteriaIndex) => (\n                    <CriteriaItem key={`criteria-${criteriaIndex}`}>\n                      <ListItemIcon>\n                        <CriteriaIcon fontSize=\"small\" color=\"primary\" />\n                      </ListItemIcon>\n                      <ListItemText\n                        primary={criteria.criteria_id}\n                        secondary={\n                          <>\n                            {criteria.criteria}\n                            <Typography\n                              component=\"span\"\n                              variant=\"body2\"\n                              color=\"primary\"\n                              sx={{ display: 'block', mt: 0.5 }}\n                            >\n                              {criteria.points} points\n                            </Typography>\n                          </>\n                        }\n                      />\n                    </CriteriaItem>\n                  ))}\n                </List>\n              )}\n            </Box>\n          ))}\n        </CardContent>\n      </Collapse>\n      \n      <Divider />\n      \n      <CardActions sx={{ justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>\n        <Tooltip title=\"Dismiss suggestion\">\n          <IconButton onClick={handleDismiss} size=\"small\">\n            <CloseIcon />\n          </IconButton>\n        </Tooltip>\n        \n        <Button\n          variant=\"contained\"\n          color=\"primary\"\n          startIcon={<CheckIcon />}\n          onClick={handleApply}\n        >\n          Apply Suggestion\n        </Button>\n      </CardActions>\n    </SuggestionCard>\n  );\n};\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nAISuggestionCard.propTypes = {\n  rubric: PropTypes.object.isRequired,\n  onApply: PropTypes.func.isRequired,\n  onDismiss: PropTypes.func.isRequired,\n};\n\nexport default AISuggestionCard;\n```\n\n### 4. Grading Mode Select Component (`/src/components/GradingModeSelect.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Grading Mode Select Component for BU MET Autograder\n * Dropdown component for selecting grading modes\n */\n\nimport React from 'react';\nimport {\n  FormControl,\n  FormHelperText,\n  InputLabel,\n  MenuItem,\n  Select,\n  Tooltip,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  Assignment as AssignmentIcon,\n  AssignmentTurnedIn as GradedIcon,\n  AssignmentLate as UngradedIcon,\n  People as SpecificIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Styled components\nconst StyledMenuItem = styled(MenuItem)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  alignItems: 'center',\n  gap: theme.spacing(1),\n}));\n\n// Grading mode descriptions\nconst modeDescriptions = {\n  ungraded: 'Grade all ungraded responses for the selected assignment or question',\n  all: 'Grade or regrade all responses (will overwrite existing grades)',\n  specific: 'Grade only selected student responses',\n};\n\n// Grading Mode Select component\nconst GradingModeSelect = ({ value, onChange, disabled = false }) => {\n  return (\n    <FormControl fullWidth variant=\"outlined\">\n      <InputLabel id=\"grading-mode-select-label\">Grading Mode</InputLabel>\n      <Select\n        labelId=\"grading-mode-select-label\"\n        value={value}\n        onChange={(e) => onChange(e.target.value)}\n        label=\"Grading Mode\"\n        disabled={disabled}\n      >\n        <StyledMenuItem value=\"ungraded\">\n          <UngradedIcon color=\"warning\" />\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\">Ungraded Responses</Typography>\n        </StyledMenuItem>\n        \n        <StyledMenuItem value=\"all\">\n          <GradedIcon color=\"primary\" />\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\">All Responses</Typography>\n        </StyledMenuItem>\n        \n        <StyledMenuItem value=\"specific\">\n          <SpecificIcon color=\"info\" />\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\">Specific Students</Typography>\n        </StyledMenuItem>\n      </Select>\n      \n      <Tooltip title={modeDescriptions[value] || ''} placement=\"right\">\n        <FormHelperText>{modeDescriptions[value]}</FormHelperText>\n      </Tooltip>\n    </FormControl>\n  );\n};\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nGradingModeSelect.propTypes = {\n  value: PropTypes.oneOf(['ungraded', 'all', 'specific']).isRequired,\n  onChange: PropTypes.func.isRequired,\n  disabled: PropTypes.bool,\n};\n\nexport default GradingModeSelect;\n```\n\n### 5. Multi-Selection List Component (`/src/components/SelectableList.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Selectable List Component for BU MET Autograder\n * UI component for selecting multiple submissions\n */\n\nimport React, { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';\nimport {\n  Box,\n  Checkbox,\n  List,\n  ListItem,\n  ListItemButton,\n  ListItemIcon,\n  Paper,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Styled components\nconst StyledListItem = styled(ListItem)(({ theme, selected, highlighted }) => ({\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(1),\n  padding: 0,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  backgroundColor: highlighted\n    ? `${theme.palette.primary.main}15`\n    : selected\n    ? `${theme.palette.action.selected}`\n    : theme.palette.background.paper,\n  border: `1px solid ${\n    highlighted\n      ? theme.palette.primary.main\n      : selected\n      ? theme.palette.action.selected\n      : theme.palette.divider\n  }`,\n}));\n\nconst StyledListItemButton = styled(ListItemButton)(({ theme }) => ({\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  padding: theme.spacing(1.5, 2),\n}));\n\n// Multi-Selection List component\nconst SelectableList = ({\n  items,\n  keyField = 'id',\n  secondaryKeyField = null,\n  selectedItems = [],\n  onSelectionChange,\n  onItemClick,\n  highlightedItem = null,\n  selectionMode = 'none',\n  renderItem,\n}) => {\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState(selectedItems);\n  const lastSelectedIndex = useRef(-1);\n  \n  // Update selected state when selectedItems prop changes\n  useEffect(() => {\n    setSelected(selectedItems);\n  }, [selectedItems]);\n  \n  // Get unique key for an item\n  const getItemKey = (item) => {\n    if (secondaryKeyField) {\n      return `${item[keyField]}-${item[secondaryKeyField]}`;\n    }\n    return item[keyField];\n  };\n  \n  // Check if an item is selected\n  const isSelected = (item) => {\n    if (selectionMode === 'none') return false;\n    \n    const itemKey = getItemKey(item);\n    return selected.includes(itemKey);\n  };\n  \n  // Check if an item is highlighted\n  const isHighlighted = (item) => {\n    if (!highlightedItem) return false;\n    \n    return getItemKey(item) === getItemKey(highlightedItem);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle item selection\n  const handleSelection = (event, item, index) => {\n    event.stopPropagation();\n    \n    if (selectionMode === 'none') return;\n    \n    const itemKey = getItemKey(item);\n    let newSelected = [...selected];\n    \n    if (event.shiftKey && selectionMode === 'multiple' && lastSelectedIndex.current >= 0) {\n      // Handle shift+click for range selection\n      const start = Math.min(lastSelectedIndex.current, index);\n      const end = Math.max(lastSelectedIndex.current, index);\n      \n      const keysToAdd = items\n        .slice(start, end + 1)\n        .map((i) => getItemKey(i))\n        .filter((key) => !newSelected.includes(key));\n      \n      newSelected = [...newSelected, ...keysToAdd];\n    } else {\n      // Handle single item selection/deselection\n      if (newSelected.includes(itemKey)) {\n        newSelected = newSelected.filter((key) => key !== itemKey);\n      } else {\n        if (selectionMode === 'single') {\n          newSelected = [itemKey];\n        } else {\n          newSelected.push(itemKey);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    lastSelectedIndex.current = index;\n    setSelected(newSelected);\n    \n    if (onSelectionChange) {\n      onSelectionChange(newSelected);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle item click (not for selection)\n  const handleItemClick = (item) => {\n    if (onItemClick) {\n      onItemClick(item);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Paper variant=\"outlined\" sx={{ maxHeight: 600, overflow: 'auto' }}>\n      {items.length === 0 ? (\n        <Box sx={{ p: 3, textAlign: 'center' }}>\n          <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n            No items available\n          </Typography>\n        </Box>\n      ) : (\n        <List disablePadding sx={{ p: 1 }}>\n          {items.map((item, index) => {\n            const isItemSelected = isSelected(item);\n            const isItemHighlighted = isHighlighted(item);\n            \n            return (\n              <StyledListItem\n                key={getItemKey(item)}\n                selected={isItemSelected}\n                highlighted={isItemHighlighted}\n                disablePadding\n              >\n                <StyledListItemButton\n                  onClick={() => handleItemClick(item)}\n                  selected={isItemSelected}\n                >\n                  {selectionMode !== 'none' && (\n                    <ListItemIcon sx={{ minWidth: 36 }}>\n                      <Checkbox\n                        edge=\"start\"\n                        checked={isItemSelected}\n                        tabIndex={-1}\n                        disableRipple\n                        onClick={(event) => handleSelection(event, item, index)}\n                      />\n                    </ListItemIcon>\n                  )}\n                  \n                  <Box sx={{ width: '100%' }}>\n                    {renderItem ? renderItem(item) : getItemKey(item)}\n                  </Box>\n                </StyledListItemButton>\n              </StyledListItem>\n            );\n          })}\n        </List>\n      )}\n    </Paper>\n  );\n};\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nSelectableList.propTypes = {\n  items: PropTypes.array.isRequired,\n  keyField: PropTypes.string,\n  secondaryKeyField: PropTypes.string,\n  selectedItems: PropTypes.array,\n  onSelectionChange: PropTypes.func,\n  onItemClick: PropTypes.func,\n  highlightedItem: PropTypes.object,\n  selectionMode: PropTypes.oneOf(['none', 'single', 'multiple']),\n  renderItem: PropTypes.func,\n};\n\nexport default SelectableList;\n```\n\nThese components implement the Rubrics & Grading features for the BU MET Autograder. They provide:\n\n1. **Rubric Management Page** - A comprehensive interface for:\n   - Creating and editing rubrics for assignments\n   - Defining grading criteria and point allocations\n   - Setting leniency levels and grading flags\n   - Getting AI-generated rubric suggestions\n\n2. **Grading Dashboard** - A robust system for grading student submissions:\n   - Filtering responses by question, grading status, and student\n   - Multiple grading modes (ungraded, all, specific students)\n   - Detailed view of student responses and grades\n   - Batch grading capabilities\n\n3. **Supporting Components**:\n   - **AISuggestionCard** - Displays AI-generated rubric suggestions with expandable details\n   - **GradingModeSelect** - Custom dropdown for selecting different grading modes\n   - **SelectableList** - Advanced list component with multi-selection support (including shift+click)\n\nAll these components include proper error handling, loading states, and responsive design. The rubric management interface provides a tab-based navigation system for overall settings and question-specific criteria. The grading dashboard offers comprehensive filtering and selection capabilities to efficiently manage student submissions.\n\nI've also implemented validation for rubric point totals to ensure they match the maximum points specified for each question.\n\nWould you like me to make any adjustments to these components or shall we proceed to the next stage of implementation?"
                }
