                    "text": "I'll implement the Manual Submission Page for stage 6:\n\n### Manual Submission Page (`/src/pages/manual_submission.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Manual Submission Page for BU MET Autograder\n * Allows instructors to simulate student responses for testing\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\nimport { useRouter } from 'next/router';\nimport {\n  Alert,\n  AlertTitle,\n  Box,\n  Button,\n  Card,\n  CardContent,\n  CircularProgress,\n  Divider,\n  FormControl,\n  FormHelperText,\n  Grid,\n  InputLabel,\n  MenuItem,\n  Paper,\n  Select,\n  Snackbar,\n  Step,\n  StepLabel,\n  Stepper,\n  TextField,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  CloudUpload as UploadIcon,\n  Send as SendIcon,\n  CheckCircleOutline as SuccessIcon,\n  ErrorOutline as ErrorIcon,\n  ArrowBack as BackIcon,\n  ArrowForward as ForwardIcon,\n} from '@mui/icons-material';\nimport { courseService, assignmentService, responseService } from '../services/api';\nimport { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/config';\nimport CardSkeleton from '../components/CardSkeleton';\n\n// Styled components\nconst SubmissionContainer = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  maxWidth: 1000,\n  margin: '0 auto',\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n}));\n\nconst StepContent = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  marginTop: theme.spacing(3),\n  marginBottom: theme.spacing(3),\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.paper,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  boxShadow: theme.shadows[1],\n}));\n\nconst FileUploadBox = styled(Box)(({ theme }) => ({\n  border: `2px dashed ${theme.palette.divider}`,\n  borderRadius: theme.shape.borderRadius,\n  padding: theme.spacing(3),\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  cursor: 'pointer',\n  transition: 'border-color 0.2s ease-in-out',\n  backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.default,\n  '&:hover': {\n    borderColor: theme.palette.primary.main,\n  },\n}));\n\n// Steps for the submission process\nconst steps = ['Select Course', 'Select Assignment', 'Provide Response', 'Review & Submit'];\n\n// Main component\nexport default function ManualSubmission() {\n  const router = useRouter();\n  \n  // State for stepper\n  const [activeStep, setActiveStep] = useState(0);\n  \n  // State for courses and assignments\n  const [courses, setCourses] = useState([]);\n  const [assignments, setAssignments] = useState([]);\n  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState([]);\n  const [loadingCourses, setLoadingCourses] = useState(true);\n  const [loadingAssignments, setLoadingAssignments] = useState(false);\n  \n  // State for selected items\n  const [selectedCourse, setSelectedCourse] = useState({\n    courseId: '',\n    semester: '',\n  });\n  const [selectedAssignment, setSelectedAssignment] = useState('');\n  const [selectedQuestion, setSelectedQuestion] = useState('');\n  \n  // State for response data\n  const [studentIdentifier, setStudentIdentifier] = useState('');\n  const [responseType, setResponseType] = useState('text');\n  const [textResponse, setTextResponse] = useState('');\n  const [fileResponse, setFileResponse] = useState(null);\n  const [filePreview, setFilePreview] = useState('');\n  \n  // State for submission\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);\n  const [submissionResult, setSubmissionResult] = useState(null);\n  \n  // State for alerts\n  const [alertOpen, setAlertOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [alertMessage, setAlertMessage] = useState('');\n  const [alertSeverity, setAlertSeverity] = useState('success');\n  \n  // Validation state\n  const [errors, setErrors] = useState({});\n  \n  // Fetch courses on component mount\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchCourses = async () => {\n      try {\n        const coursesData = await courseService.getCourses();\n        setCourses(coursesData || []);\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error('Error fetching courses:', error);\n        setAlertMessage('Failed to load courses: ' + error.message);\n        setAlertSeverity('error');\n        setAlertOpen(true);\n      } finally {\n        setLoadingCourses(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    fetchCourses();\n  }, []);\n  \n  // Fetch assignments when course is selected\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchAssignments = async () => {\n      if (!selectedCourse.courseId || !selectedCourse.semester) return;\n      \n      setLoadingAssignments(true);\n      try {\n        const assignmentsData = await assignmentService.getAssignments(\n          selectedCourse.courseId,\n          selectedCourse.semester\n        );\n        setAssignments(assignmentsData || []);\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error('Error fetching assignments:', error);\n        setAlertMessage('Failed to load assignments: ' + error.message);\n        setAlertSeverity('error');\n        setAlertOpen(true);\n      } finally {\n        setLoadingAssignments(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    if (selectedCourse.courseId && selectedCourse.semester) {\n      fetchAssignments();\n    }\n  }, [selectedCourse]);\n  \n  // Update questions when assignment is selected\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!selectedAssignment) {\n      setQuestions([]);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    const assignment = assignments.find((a) => a.assignment_id === selectedAssignment);\n    if (assignment) {\n      setQuestions(assignment.questions || []);\n    } else {\n      setQuestions([]);\n    }\n  }, [selectedAssignment, assignments]);\n  \n  // Handle course selection\n  const handleCourseSelect = (courseId, semester) => {\n    setSelectedCourse({ courseId, semester });\n    setSelectedAssignment('');\n    setSelectedQuestion('');\n  };\n  \n  // Handle file selection\n  const handleFileSelect = (event) => {\n    const file = event.target.files[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n    \n    // Check file size\n    if (file.size > APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize) {\n      setErrors({\n        ...errors,\n        file: `File size exceeds the maximum limit of ${APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize / (1024 * 1024)}MB.`,\n      });\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Check file type\n    const fileExtension = `.${file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase()}`;\n    if (!APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.includes(fileExtension)) {\n      setErrors({\n        ...errors,\n        file: `File type not supported. Accepted types: ${APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.join(', ')}`,\n      });\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    setFileResponse(file);\n    setErrors({ ...errors, file: null });\n    \n    // Create file preview\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = (e) => {\n      setFilePreview(e.target.result);\n    };\n    reader.readAsDataURL(file);\n  };\n  \n  // Handle file drop\n  const handleFileDrop = (event) => {\n    event.preventDefault();\n    event.stopPropagation();\n    \n    if (event.dataTransfer.files && event.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {\n      const file = event.dataTransfer.files[0];\n      \n      // Check file size\n      if (file.size > APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize) {\n        setErrors({\n          ...errors,\n          file: `File size exceeds the maximum limit of ${APP_CONFIG.maxUploadSize / (1024 * 1024)}MB.`,\n        });\n        return;\n      }\n      \n      // Check file type\n      const fileExtension = `.${file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase()}`;\n      if (!APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.includes(fileExtension)) {\n        setErrors({\n          ...errors,\n          file: `File type not supported. Accepted types: ${APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.join(', ')}`,\n        });\n        return;\n      }\n      \n      setFileResponse(file);\n      setErrors({ ...errors, file: null });\n      \n      // Create file preview\n      const reader = new FileReader();\n      reader.onload = (e) => {\n        setFilePreview(e.target.result);\n      };\n      reader.readAsDataURL(file);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Prevent default drag behavior\n  const handleDragOver = (event) => {\n    event.preventDefault();\n    event.stopPropagation();\n  };\n  \n  // Handle step navigation\n  const handleNext = () => {\n    // Validate current step\n    if (!validateCurrentStep()) return;\n    \n    setActiveStep((prevStep) => prevStep + 1);\n  };\n  \n  const handleBack = () => {\n    setActiveStep((prevStep) => prevStep - 1);\n  };\n  \n  const handleReset = () => {\n    setActiveStep(0);\n    setSelectedCourse({ courseId: '', semester: '' });\n    setSelectedAssignment('');\n    setSelectedQuestion('');\n    setStudentIdentifier('');\n    setResponseType('text');\n    setTextResponse('');\n    setFileResponse(null);\n    setFilePreview('');\n    setSubmissionResult(null);\n    setErrors({});\n  };\n  \n  // Validate current step\n  const validateCurrentStep = () => {\n    let isValid = true;\n    const newErrors = {};\n    \n    switch (activeStep) {\n      case 0: // Course selection\n        if (!selectedCourse.courseId || !selectedCourse.semester) {\n          newErrors.course = 'Please select a course';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        break;\n        \n      case 1: // Assignment selection\n        if (!selectedAssignment) {\n          newErrors.assignment = 'Please select an assignment';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        if (!selectedQuestion) {\n          newErrors.question = 'Please select a question';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        break;\n        \n      case 2: // Response data\n        if (!studentIdentifier) {\n          newErrors.studentIdentifier = 'Please enter a student identifier';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        \n        if (responseType === 'text' && !textResponse.trim()) {\n          newErrors.textResponse = 'Please enter a response';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        \n        if (responseType === 'file' && !fileResponse) {\n          newErrors.file = 'Please upload a file';\n          isValid = false;\n        }\n        break;\n        \n      default:\n        break;\n    }\n    \n    setErrors(newErrors);\n    return isValid;\n  };\n  \n  // Handle submission\n  const handleSubmit = async () => {\n    if (!validateCurrentStep()) return;\n    \n    setSubmitting(true);\n    \n    try {\n      // Prepare response data\n      let responseData;\n      \n      if (responseType === 'text') {\n        responseData = {\n          student_id: studentIdentifier,\n          assignment_id: selectedAssignment,\n          question_index: parseInt(selectedQuestion),\n          data: {\n            data_type: '.txt',\n            content: btoa(textResponse), // Base64 encode the text\n          },\n        };\n      } else {\n        // Read file as base64\n        const fileContent = await readFileAsBase64(fileResponse);\n        \n        responseData = {\n          student_id: studentIdentifier,\n          assignment_id: selectedAssignment,\n          question_index: parseInt(selectedQuestion),\n          data: {\n            data_type: `.${fileResponse.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase()}`,\n            content: fileContent,\n            metadata: {\n              filename: fileResponse.name,\n              size: `${(fileResponse.size / 1024).toFixed(2)}KB`,\n              type: fileResponse.type,\n            },\n          },\n        };\n      }\n      \n      // Submit response\n      await responseService.uploadResponse(responseData);\n      \n      setSubmissionResult({\n        success: true,\n        message: 'Response submitted successfully!',\n      });\n      \n      setAlertMessage('Response submitted successfully!');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error submitting response:', error);\n      \n      setSubmissionResult({\n        success: false,\n        message: `Submission failed: ${error.message}`,\n      });\n      \n      setAlertMessage(`Submission failed: ${error.message}`);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Helper function to read file as base64\n  const readFileAsBase64 = (file) => {\n    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n      const reader = new FileReader();\n      reader.onload = () => {\n        // Extract the base64 content from the data URL\n        const base64Content = reader.result.split(',')[1];\n        resolve(base64Content);\n      };\n      reader.onerror = (error) => reject(error);\n      reader.readAsDataURL(file);\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Render step content\n  const getStepContent = (step) => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 0: // Course selection\n        return (\n          <StepContent>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              Select a Course\n            </Typography>\n            \n            {loadingCourses ? (\n              <Box sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n                <CardSkeleton height={100} />\n                <CardSkeleton height={100} />\n              </Box>\n            ) : courses.length === 0 ? (\n              <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                No courses available. Please create a course first.\n              </Alert>\n            ) : (\n              <Grid container spacing={3} sx={{ mt: 1 }}>\n                {courses.map((course) => (\n                  <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} key={`${course.course_id}-${course.semester}`}>\n                    <Card\n                      raised={\n                        selectedCourse.courseId === course.course_id &&\n                        selectedCourse.semester === course.semester\n                      }\n                      sx={{\n                        cursor: 'pointer',\n                        transition: 'transform 0.2s',\n                        '&:hover': {\n                          transform: 'translateY(-4px)',\n                        },\n                      }}\n                      onClick={() => handleCourseSelect(course.course_id, course.semester)}\n                    >\n                      <CardContent>\n                        <Typography variant=\"h6\" noWrap>\n                          {course.course_id}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          {course.semester}\n                        </Typography>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" sx={{ mt: 1 }}>\n                          {course.instructors?.length} {course.instructors?.length === 1 ? 'instructor' : 'instructors'}\n                        </Typography>\n                      </CardContent>\n                    </Card>\n                  </Grid>\n                ))}\n              </Grid>\n            )}\n            \n            {errors.course && (\n              <Alert severity=\"error\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                {errors.course}\n              </Alert>\n            )}\n          </StepContent>\n        );\n        \n      case 1: // Assignment selection\n        return (\n          <StepContent>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              Select an Assignment and Question\n            </Typography>\n            \n            {loadingAssignments ? (\n              <Box sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n                <CardSkeleton height={100} />\n              </Box>\n            ) : assignments.length === 0 ? (\n              <Alert severity=\"info\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                No assignments available for this course. Please create an assignment first.\n              </Alert>\n            ) : (\n              <Box sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n                <FormControl fullWidth error={!!errors.assignment} sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n                  <InputLabel id=\"assignment-select-label\">Assignment</InputLabel>\n                  <Select\n                    labelId=\"assignment-select-label\"\n                    value={selectedAssignment}\n                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedAssignment(e.target.value)}\n                    label=\"Assignment\"\n                  >\n                    {assignments.map((assignment) => (\n                      <MenuItem key={assignment.assignment_id} value={assignment.assignment_id}>\n                        {assignment.assignment_title || `Assignment ${assignment.assignment_id}`}\n                      </MenuItem>\n                    ))}\n                  </Select>\n                  {errors.assignment && <FormHelperText>{errors.assignment}</FormHelperText>}\n                </FormControl>\n                \n                <FormControl fullWidth error={!!errors.question} disabled={!selectedAssignment}>\n                  <InputLabel id=\"question-select-label\">Question</InputLabel>\n                  <Select\n                    labelId=\"question-select-label\"\n                    value={selectedQuestion}\n                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedQuestion(e.target.value)}\n                    label=\"Question\"\n                  >\n                    {questions.map((question) => (\n                      <MenuItem key={question.question_index} value={question.question_index}>\n                        Question {question.question_index + 1}\n                      </MenuItem>\n                    ))}\n                  </Select>\n                  {errors.question && <FormHelperText>{errors.question}</FormHelperText>}\n                </FormControl>\n                \n                {selectedAssignment && selectedQuestion !== '' && (\n                  <Paper sx={{ p: 2, mt: 3, bgcolor: 'background.default' }}>\n                    <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                      Question Preview:\n                    </Typography>\n                    <Typography variant=\"body1\">\n                      {\n                        questions.find(\n                          (q) => q.question_index === parseInt(selectedQuestion)\n                        )?.question_text\n                      }\n                    </Typography>\n                  </Paper>\n                )}\n              </Box>\n            )}\n          </StepContent>\n        );\n        \n      case 2: // Response data\n        return (\n          <StepContent>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              Provide Response Data\n            </Typography>\n            \n            <TextField\n              label=\"Student Identifier\"\n              fullWidth\n              margin=\"normal\"\n              value={studentIdentifier}\n              onChange={(e) => setStudentIdentifier(e.target.value)}\n              error={!!errors.studentIdentifier}\n              helperText={\n                errors.studentIdentifier ||\n                \"Enter a unique identifier for the student (e.g., email, ID number)\"\n              }\n            />\n            \n            <FormControl fullWidth margin=\"normal\">\n              <InputLabel id=\"response-type-label\">Response Type</InputLabel>\n              <Select\n                labelId=\"response-type-label\"\n                value={responseType}\n                onChange={(e) => setResponseType(e.target.value)}\n                label=\"Response Type\"\n              >\n                <MenuItem value=\"text\">Text Response</MenuItem>\n                <MenuItem value=\"file\">File Upload</MenuItem>\n              </Select>\n              <FormHelperText>\n                Select how you want to provide the response\n              </FormHelperText>\n            </FormControl>\n            \n            {responseType === 'text' ? (\n              <TextField\n                label=\"Text Response\"\n                fullWidth\n                multiline\n                rows={6}\n                margin=\"normal\"\n                value={textResponse}\n                onChange={(e) => setTextResponse(e.target.value)}\n                error={!!errors.textResponse}\n                helperText={errors.textResponse}\n                placeholder=\"Enter the student's response text here...\"\n              />\n            ) : (\n              <Box sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n                <input\n                  type=\"file\"\n                  id=\"file-upload\"\n                  style={{ display: 'none' }}\n                  onChange={handleFileSelect}\n                  accept={APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.join(',')}\n                />\n                \n                <FileUploadBox\n                  component=\"label\"\n                  htmlFor=\"file-upload\"\n                  onDrop={handleFileDrop}\n                  onDragOver={handleDragOver}\n                  sx={{ borderColor: errors.file ? 'error.main' : 'divider' }}\n                >\n                  <UploadIcon fontSize=\"large\" color=\"primary\" />\n                  <Typography variant=\"h6\" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>\n                    {fileResponse ? 'File Selected' : 'Drag & Drop or Click to Upload'}\n                  </Typography>\n                  {fileResponse ? (\n                    <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                      {fileResponse.name} ({(fileResponse.size / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB)\n                    </Typography>\n                  ) : (\n                    <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                      Accepted file types: {APP_CONFIG.acceptedFileTypes.submissions.join(', ')}\n                    </Typography>\n                  )}\n                </FileUploadBox>\n                \n                {errors.file && (\n                  <Typography color=\"error\" variant=\"body2\" sx={{ mt: 1 }}>\n                    {errors.file}\n                  </Typography>\n                )}\n                \n                {fileResponse && filePreview && (\n                  <Box sx={{ mt: 3 }}>\n                    <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" gutterBottom>\n                      File Preview:\n                    </Typography>\n                    {fileResponse.type.startsWith('image/') ? (\n                      <Box\n                        component=\"img\"\n                        src={filePreview}\n                        alt=\"File preview\"\n                        sx={{\n                          maxWidth: '100%',\n                          maxHeight: 200,\n                          objectFit: 'contain',\n                          border: (theme) => `1px solid ${theme.palette.divider}`,\n                          borderRadius: 1,\n                        }}\n                      />\n                    ) : (\n                      <Paper sx={{ p: 2, bgcolor: 'background.default' }}>\n                        <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n                          Preview not available for this file type.\n                        </Typography>\n                      </Paper>\n                    )}\n                  </Box>\n                )}\n              </Box>\n            )}\n          </StepContent>\n        );\n        \n      case 3: // Review & Submit\n        return (\n          <StepContent>\n            <Typography variant=\"h6\" gutterBottom>\n              Review & Submit\n            </Typography>\n            \n            <Grid container spacing={3}>\n              <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>\n                <Paper sx={{ p: 2 }}>\n                  <Typography variant=\"subtitle1\" fontWeight=\"bold\" gutterBottom>\n                    Course Information\n                  </Typography>\n                  <Typography variant=\"body2\">\n                    <strong>Course ID:</strong> {selectedCourse.courseId}\n                  </Typography>\n                  <Typography variant=\"body2\">\n                    <strong>Semester:</strong> <strong>Assignment:</strong>{' '}\n                    {\n                      assignments.find((a) => a.assignment_id === selectedAssignment)\n                        ?.assignment_title || 'Success' : 'Error'}</AlertTitle>\n                {submissionResult.message}\n              </Alert>\n            )}\n          </StepContent>\n        );\n        \n      default:\n        return 'Unknown step';\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Render navigation buttons\n  const renderNavButtons = () => {\n    return (\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', mt: 3 }}>\n        <Button\n          variant=\"outlined\"\n          disabled={activeStep === 0 || submitting}\n          onClick={handleBack}\n          startIcon={<BackIcon />}\n        >\n          Back\n        </Button>\n        \n        <Box>\n          {activeStep === steps.length - 1 ? 'Submitting...' : 'Submit Response'}\n            </Button>\n          ) : (\n            <Button\n              variant=\"contained\"\n              color=\"primary\"\n              onClick={handleNext}\n              endIcon={<ForwardIcon />}\n            >\n              Next\n            </Button>\n          )}\n          \n          {submissionResult?.success && (\n            <Button\n              variant=\"outlined\"\n              color=\"primary\"\n              onClick={handleReset}\n              sx={{ ml: 2 }}\n            >\n              Submit Another\n            </Button>\n          )}\n        </Box>\n      </Box>\n    );\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <SubmissionContainer>\n      <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\" gutterBottom>\n        Manual Student Submission\n      </Typography>\n      \n      <Typography variant=\"body1\" color=\"text.secondary\" paragraph>\n        Use this tool to simulate student responses for testing the grading system.\n      </Typography>\n      \n      <Stepper activeStep={activeStep} sx={{ my: 4 }}>\n        {steps.map((label) => (\n          <Step key={label}>\n            <StepLabel>{label}</StepLabel>\n          </Step>\n        ))}\n      </Stepper>\n      \n      {getStepContent(activeStep)}\n      \n      {renderNavButtons()}\n      \n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </SubmissionContainer>\n  );\n}\n```\n\nThis Manual Submission Page provides a comprehensive interface for instructors to simulate student responses for testing purposes. Here's what it includes:\n\n1. **Step-by-Step Wizard:**\n   - A guided, multi-step process with clear navigation\n   - Steps for selecting course, assignment, providing response data, and reviewing/submitting\n\n2. **Course & Assignment Selection:**\n   - Visual selection of courses with semester information\n   - Dropdown selection for assignments and questions\n   - Preview of the selected question\n\n3. **Response Input Options:**\n   - Text response input with a multi-line text field\n   - File upload with drag-and-drop support\n   - File previews when applicable\n   - Input validation for required fields and file restrictions\n\n4. **Review & Submit:**\n   - Comprehensive summary of all selections before submission\n   - Clear feedback on submission status\n   - Option to submit another response after successful submission\n\n5. **Error Handling & Validation:**\n   - Validation at each step to ensure all required data is provided\n   - File size and type validation according to application settings\n   - Error messages displayed inline with the relevant fields\n   - Alert notifications for API errors\n\n6. **User Experience Features:**\n   - Loading states for asynchronous operations\n   - Skeleton loaders during data fetching\n   - Responsive design for all screen sizes\n   - Helpful guidance text throughout the form\n\nThe page implements a robust file upload mechanism with support for both click-to-upload and drag-and-drop, including validation of file types and sizes according to the application configuration. Tabs,\n  TextField,\n  Tooltip,\n  Typography,\n} from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport {\n  AccountCircle as AccountIcon,\n  Add as AddIcon,\n  ContentCopy as Main component\nexport default function Settings() {\n  // Theme context\n  const { mode, toggleTheme } = useTheme();\n  \n  // Tab state\n  const [tabValue, setTabValue] = useState(0);\n  \n  // User setLoadingTokens(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Fetch tokens when API tab is selected\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (tabValue === 1) {\n      fetchTokens();\n    }\n  }, [tabValue]);\n  \n  // Handle e.target;\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      [name]: value,\n    });\n  };\n  \n  // Handle dark mode toggle\n  const handleDarkModeToggle = () => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      dark_mode: !formData.dark_mode,\n    });\n    \n    // Also toggle the theme in the context (for immediate visual feedback)\n    toggleTheme();\n  };\n  \n  // Handle form submission\n  const setAlertMessage('Profile updated successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error updating profile:', error);\n      setAlertMessage('Failed to update profile: ' + error.message);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } finally {\n      setSaving(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle token creation\n  const handleCreateToken = async () => {\n    try {\n      const token = await authService.createToken(newTokenName);\n      setNewToken(token);\n      setNewTokenName('');\n      setCreateTokenDialogOpen(false);\n      \n      // Refresh tokens list\n      await fetchTokens();\n      \n      setAlertMessage('Token created successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error creating token:', error);\n      setAlertMessage('Failed to create token: ' + error.message);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle token deletion\n  const handleDeleteToken = async () => {\n    if (!tokenToDelete) return;\n    \n    try {\n      await authService.deleteToken(tokenToDelete.token_id);\n      \n      // Remove token from list\n      setTokens(tokens.filter((t) => t.token_id !== tokenToDelete.token_id));\n      \n      setAlertMessage('Token deleted successfully');\n      setAlertSeverity('success');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error deleting token:', error);\n      setAlertMessage('Failed to delete token: ' + error.message);\n      setAlertSeverity('error');\n      setAlertOpen(true);\n    } finally {\n      setTokenToDelete(null);\n      setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Handle copying token to clipboard\n  const handleCopyToken = (token) => {\n    navigator.clipboard.writeText(token);\n    setAlertMessage('Token copied to clipboard');\n    setAlertSeverity('success');\n    setAlertOpen(true);\n  };\n  \n  // Render profile settings tab\n  const renderProfileSettings = () => {\n    if (loading) {\n      return     </Grid>\n            \n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6}>\n              <TextField\n                label=\"Last Name\"\n                name=\"last_name\"\n    </Grid>\n            \n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6}>\n              <TextField\n                label=\"Email\"\n                value={userData?.user_email || ''}\n                fullWidth\n                margin=\"normal\"\n                variant=\"outlined\"\n                disabled\n                helperText=\"Email cannot be changed\"\n              />\n            </Grid>\n            \n            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6}>\n              <Paper\n                sx={{\n                  p: 2,\n                  mt: 2,\n                  display: 'flex',\n                     {token.token_name}\n                          </Typography>\n                          \n                          <Typography variant=\"body2\" color=\"text.secondary\">\n               </IconButton>\n                        </Tooltip>\n                      </Box>\n                    </Box>\n                  </TokenCard>\n                ))}\n              </List>\n            )}\n            \n            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end', mt: 2 }}>\n              <Button\n                startIcon={<RefreshIcon />}\n                onClick={fetchTokens}\n                disabled={loadingTokens}\n              >\n                Refresh\n              </Button>\n            </Box>\n          </CardContent>\n        </SettingsCard>\n        \n        {/* Display new token after creation */}\n        {newToken && (\n          <SettingsCard>\n            <CardHeader\n              title={<Typography variant=\"h6\">New Token Created</Typography>}\n              subheader=\"This token will only be shown once. Please copy it now.\"\n            />\n            \n            <CardContent>\n              <Alert severity=\"warning\" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>\n                Make sure to copy this token now. For security reasons, it won't be displayed again.\n              </Alert>\n              \n              <Paper\n                sx={{\n                  p: 2,\n                  display: 'flex',\n                  alignItems: 'center',\n                  justifyContent: 'space-between',\n                  bgcolor: 'background.default',\n                }}\n              >\n                <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexGrow: 1, overflow: 'hidden' }}>\n                  <Typography\n                    variant=\"body2\"\n                    fontFamily=\"monospace\"\n                    sx={{\n                      overflow: 'hidden',\n                      textOverflow: 'ellipsis',\n                      whiteSpace: 'nowrap',\n                    }}\n                  >\n                    {showToken ? newToken.token_id : '••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••'}\n                  </Typography>\n                </Box>\n                \n                <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', ml: 2 }}>\n                  <Tooltip title={showToken ? 'Hide Token' : 'Show Token'}>\n                    <IconButton onClick={() => setShowToken(!showToken)} size=\"small\">\n                      {showToken ? <VisibilityOffIcon /> : <VisibilityIcon />}\n                    </IconButton>\n                  </Tooltip>\n                  \n                  <Tooltip title=\"Copy to Clipboard\">\n                    <IconButton\n                      onClick={() => handleCopyToken(newToken.token_id)}\n                      color=\"primary\"\n                      size=\"small\"\n                    >\n                      <CopyIcon />\n                    </IconButton>\n                  </Tooltip>\n                </Box>\n              </Paper>\n              \n              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end', mt: 2 }}>\n                <Button\n                  variant=\"contained\"\n                  onClick={() => setNewToken(null)}\n                >\n                  I've Copied My Token\n                </Button>\n              </Box>\n            </CardContent>\n          </SettingsCard>\n        )}\n      </>\n    );\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <SettingsContainer>\n      <Typography variant=\"h4\" component=\"h1\" gutterBottom>\n        Settings\n      </Typography>\n      \n      <Paper sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n        <Tabs\n          value={tabValue}\n          onChange={handleTabChange}\n          variant=\"fullWidth\"\n          aria-label=\"settings tabs\"\n        >\n          <Tab\n            label=\"Profile\"\n            icon={<AccountIcon />}\n            iconPosition=\"start\"\n          />\n          <Tab\n            label=\"API Tokens\"\n            icon={<KeyIcon />}\n            iconPosition=\"start\"\n          />\n        </Tabs>\n      </Paper>\n      \n      <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={0}>\n        {renderProfileSettings()}\n      </TabPanel>\n      \n      <TabPanel value={tabValue} index={1}>\n        {renderAPITokens()}\n      </TabPanel>\n      \n      {/* Create Token Dialog */}\n      <Dialog\n        open={createTokenDialogOpen}\n        onClose={() => setCreateTokenDialogOpen(false)}\n        maxWidth=\"sm\"\n        fullWidth\n      >\n        <DialogTitle>Create New API Token</DialogTitle>\n        <DialogContent>\n          <DialogContentText>\n            API tokens allow programmatic access to the BU MET Autograder API. Tokens should be kept\n            secure and not shared with others.\n          </DialogContentText>\n          \n          <TextField\n            autoFocus\n            margin=\"dense\"\n            label=\"Token Name\"\n            fullWidth\n            variant=\"outlined\"\n            value={newTokenName}\n            onChange={(e) => setNewTokenName(e.target.value)}\n            placeholder=\"e.g., Development, Testing, etc.\"\n            sx={{ mt: 2 }}\n          />\n        </DialogContent>\n        \n        <DialogActions>\n          <Button onClick={() => setCreateTokenDialogOpen(false)}>\n            Cancel\n          </Button>\n          <Button\n            onClick={handleCreateToken}\n            variant=\"contained\"\n            color=\"primary\"\n            disabled={!newTokenName.trim()}\n          >\n            Create\n          </Button>\n        </DialogActions>\n      </Dialog>\n      \n      {/* Delete Token Confirmation Dialog */}\n      <ConfirmationDialog\n        open={deleteDialogOpen}\n        title=\"Delete API Token\"\n        message={`Are you sure you want to delete the token \"${tokenToDelete?.token_name}\"? This action cannot be undone.`}\n        confirmText=\"Delete\"\n        cancelText=\"Cancel\"\n        confirmButtonProps={{ color: 'error' }}\n        onConfirm={handleDeleteToken}\n        onCancel={() => {\n          setDeleteDialogOpen(false);\n          setTokenToDelete(null);\n        }}\n      />\n      \n      {/* Alert Snackbar */}\n      <Snackbar\n        open={alertOpen}\n        autoHideDuration={6000}\n        onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n        anchorOrigin={{ vertical: 'bottom', horizontal: 'center' }}\n      >\n        <Alert\n          onClose={() => setAlertOpen(false)}\n          severity={alertSeverity}\n          variant=\"filled\"\n          sx={{ width: '100%' }}\n        >\n          {alertMessage}\n        </Alert>\n      </Snackbar>\n    </SettingsContainer>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Skeleton Loader Component (`/src/components/CardSkeleton.js`)\n\n```jsx\n/**\n * Card Skeleton Component for BU MET Autograder\n * Provides placeholder loading states for better UX\n */\n\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Box, Card, CardContent, Skeleton } from '@mui/material';\nimport { styled } from '@mui/material/styles';\nimport PropTypes from 'prop-types';\n\n// Styled components\nconst StyledCard = styled(Card)(({ theme }) => ({\n  height: '100%',\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n}));\n\nconst SkeletonContainer = styled(CardContent)(({ theme }) => ({\n  display: 'flex',\n  flexDirection: 'column',\n  flexGrow: 1,\n}));\n\n// CardSkeleton component\nconst CardSkeleton = ({\n  height = 200,\n  animation = 'pulse',\n  variant = 'rectangular',\n  count = 1,\n}) => {\n  // Generate multiple skeletons if count > 1\n  if (count > 1) {\n    return (\n      <Box sx={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fill, minmax(300px, 1fr))', gap: 2 }}>\n        {Array.from(new Array(count)).map((_, index) => (\n          <CardSkeleton\n            key={index}\n            height={height}\n            animation={animation}\n            variant={variant}\n            count={1}\n          />\n        ))}\n      </Box>\n    );\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <StyledCard>\n      <SkeletonContainer>\n        <Skeleton\n          variant=\"text\"\n          animation={animation}\n          height={28}\n          width=\"60%\"\n          sx={{ mb: 1 }}\n        />\n        <Skeleton\n          variant=\"text\"\n          animation={animation}\n          height={20}\n          width=\"40%\"\n          sx={{ mb: 2 }}\n        />\n        <Skeleton\n          variant={variant}\n          animation={animation}\n          height={height - 100 > 0 ? height - 100 : 20}\n          sx={{ mb: 1, flexGrow: 1 }}\n        />\n        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', mt: 'auto' }}>\n          <Skeleton\n            variant=\"text\"\n            animation={animation}\n            height={20}\n            width=\"30%\"\n          />\n          <Skeleton\n            variant=\"rounded\"\n            animation={animation}\n            height={36}\n            width=\"20%\"\n          />\n        </Box>\n      </SkeletonContainer>\n    </StyledCard>\n  );\n};\n\n// PropTypes for type checking\nCardSkeleton.propTypes = {\n  height: PropTypes.number,\n  animation: PropTypes.oneOf(['pulse', 'wave', false]),\n  variant: PropTypes.oneOf(['text', 'rectangular', 'rounded', 'circular']),\n  count: PropTypes.number,\n};\n\nexport default CardSkeleton;\n```\n\n### 3. Public Assets\n\n#### a. `/public/robots.txt`\n\n```\n# BU MET Autograder robots.txt\nUser-agent: *\nAllow: /\n\n# Disallow sensitive routes\nDisallow: /settings\nDisallow: /course/*/grading\nDisallow: /manual_submission\n\n# Sitemap\nSitemap: https://autograder.bu.edu/sitemap.xml\n```\n\n#### b. `/public/images/` Directory Structure\n\n```\n/public/images/\n├── bu-logo.png             # Boston University logo\n├── bu-met-logo.png         # BU Metropolitan College logo\n├── avatar-placeholder.png  # Default user avatar placeholder\n├── login-background.jpg    # Background image for login page\n└── favicon.png             # Favicon source image\n```\n\n#### c. `/public/icons/` Directory Structure\n\n```\n/public/icons/\n├── favicon.ico             # 16x16 favicon\n├── icon-192x192.png        # 192x192 PWA icon\n├── icon-512x512.png        # 512x512 PWA icon\n├── apple-touch-icon.png    # 180x180 Apple touch icon\n└── manifest-icon.png       # Icon for manifest.json\n```\n\n### 4. A comprehensive settings interface with:\n   - Profile management (name, dark mode preferences)\n   - API token management (creation, viewing, deletion)\n   - Secure token handling with copy-to-clipboard functionality\n\n2. **CardSkeleton Component** - Next.js configuration with image optimization, redirects, and environment variables\n\nThe Settings page provides a complete user profile and API token management system with appropriate security measures, such as showing tokens only once and requiring confirmation for deletion. The CardSkeleton component enhances user experience by providing visual feedback during loading states throughout the application."
